# Surface Reconstruction From Point Clouds: A Survey and a Benchmark

# Introduction

**Surface reconstruction** t·ª´ point clouds l√† m·ªôt b√†i to√°n l√¢u ƒë·ªùi trong lƒ©nh v·ª±c computer vision v√† computer graphics. Point cloud l√† t·∫≠p h·ª£p c√°c ƒëi·ªÉm r·ªùi r·∫°c `discrete` trong kh√¥ng gian 3D ƒë∆∞·ª£c thu th·∫≠p t·ª´ c√°c c·∫£m bi·∫øn nh∆∞ **multi-view stereo**, **structured light**, ho·∫∑c **time-of-flight (ToF)**. Tuy nhi√™n, b√†i to√°n n√†y g·∫∑p nhi·ªÅu th·ª≠ th√°ch `challenges` do:

- *Ill-posed problem*: V·ªõi m·ªói point cloud, c√≥ v√¥ s·ªë [**Continuous Surface**](https://www.notion.so/Continuous-Surface-1462a3f8f2a180189662e5f1362945b4?pvs=21)  c√≥ th·ªÉ ph√π h·ª£p.
- *Imperfections*: D·ªØ li·ªáu Point Cloud th∆∞·ªùng c√≥ nhi·ªÖu (noise), ph√¢n b·ªë kh√¥ng ƒë·ªìng ƒë·ªÅu (non-uniform distribution), ho·∫∑c ch·ª©a c√°c outliers.

**M·ª•c ti√™u c·ªßa b√†i b√°o**:

- ƒê√°nh gi√° c√°c ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p surface reconstruction hi·ªán c√≥, bao g·ªìm c·∫£ ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p c·ªï ƒëi·ªÉn `classical` v√† hi·ªán ƒë·∫°i `deep learning`.
- X√¢y d·ª±ng m·ªôt b·ªô dataset **benchmark** to√†n di·ªán, bao g·ªìm d·ªØ li·ªáu t·ªïng h·ª£p `synthetic` v√† d·ªØ li·ªáu th·ª±c t·∫ø `real-scanned`, c·ª• th·ªÉ `object-` v√† `scene-level` surfaces.
- Ph√¢n t√≠ch chi ti·∫øt ∆∞u, nh∆∞·ª£c ƒëi·ªÉm c·ªßa c√°c ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p hi·ªán c√≥ th√¥ng qua th·ª±c nghi·ªám.

**ƒê√°nh gi√° t√°c gi·∫£:**

- C√°c v·∫•n ƒë·ªÅ v·ªÅ `misaligment`, `missing points`, `outliers` √≠t ƒë∆∞·ª£c quan t√¢m v√† ch∆∞a c√≥ l·ªùi gi·∫£i
- C√°c ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p deep Learning th·ªÉ hi·ªán t·ªët v√† ti·ªÅm nƒÉng cho surface modeling v√† reconstruction. Tuy nhi√™n, nghi√™n c·ª©u t√°c gi·∫£ ƒë·ªÅ xu·∫•t c√°c ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p hi·ªán ƒë·∫°i kh√¥ng generalization t·ªët trong vi·ªác t√°i t·∫°o c√°c b·ªÅ m·∫∑t ph·ª©c t·∫°p. Nhi·ªÅu ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p classical t·ªët h∆°n c·∫£ v·ªÅ m·∫∑t `generlization` v√† `robustness`

- S·ª≠ d·ª•ng ph√°p tuy·∫øn  [**Normal**](https://www.notion.so/Normal-1462a3f8f2a180eb82a1e9cf965039f7?pvs=21) l√† quan tr·ªçng trong task surface reconstruction t·ª´ c√°c `raw`, `observed` point clouds. Ngay c·∫£ khi normal ƒë∆∞·ª£c x√°c ƒë·ªãnh k√©m ch√≠nh x√°c, k·∫øt qu·∫£ interior/exterior b·ªÅ m·∫∑t v·∫´n c√≥ th·ªÉ x√°c ƒë·ªãnh t·ªët trong kh√¥ng gian 3D.

# Problem Statement

Cho m·ªôt t·∫≠p h·ª£p ƒëi·ªÉm r·ªùi r·∫°c `discrete point` $P = \{p \in \mathbb{R}^3\}$, ƒë·∫°i di·ªán cho c√°c ƒëi·ªÉm tr√™n b·ªÅ m·∫∑t ƒë∆∞·ª£c scan b·ªüi c·∫£m bi·∫øn 3D. Nhi·ªám v·ª• l√† t√¨m m·ªôt **[**Continuous Surface**](https://www.notion.so/Continuous-Surface-1462a3f8f2a180189662e5f1362945b4?pvs=21) $S^*$** sao cho:

1. **Reconstruct surface** $S^*$ kh·ªõp v·ªõi t·∫≠p d·ªØ li·ªáu input $P$.
2. $S^*$ th·ªèa m√£n c√°c r√†ng bu·ªôc v·ªÅ h√¨nh h·ªçc `geometry-aware constraints`. (e.g., [Smooth Surface](https://www.notion.so/Smooth-Surface-1462a3f8f2a1804b9930e23513f1fcad?pvs=21))

Tuy nhi√™n, b√†i to√°n n√†y l√† **`ill-posed`**, v√¨ c√≥ v√¥ s·ªë b·ªÅ m·∫∑t $S^*$ c√≥ th·ªÉ ph√π h·ª£p v·ªõi $P$. ƒê·ªÉ kh·∫Øc ph·ª•c, c·∫ßn √°p d·ª•ng regularization ƒë·ªÉ t√¨m surface $S$ tho·∫£ m√£n c·∫£ **kh·ªõp d·ªØ li·ªáu** v√† **ƒë·∫∑c t√≠nh h√¨nh h·ªçc.**

B√†i to√°n ƒë∆∞·ª£c bi·ªÉu di·ªÖn b·∫±ng m·ªôt c√¥ng th·ª©c t·ªëi ∆∞u ho√° t·ªïng qu√°t `regularized optimization`:

$$
\min_{S} \mathcal{L}(S; P) + \lambda \mathcal{R}(S)
$$

Trong ƒë√≥:

- $\mathcal{L}(S; P)$: H√†m **Loss** ([**Data Fidelity**](https://www.notion.so/Data-Fidelity-1442a3f8f2a180bcbfdef563f8d1ceb7?pvs=21)), ƒëo ƒë·ªô sai l·ªách gi·ªØa surface $S$ v√† d·ªØ li·ªáu $P$.
- $\mathcal{R}(S)$: **Regularizer**, th√™m r√†ng bu·ªôc ƒë·ªÉ ki·ªÉm so√°t h√¨nh h·ªçc c·ªßa $S$
- $\lambda$: **Scalar penalty**, h·ªá s·ªë ƒëi·ªÅu ch·ªânh m·ª©c ƒë·ªô ∆∞u ti√™n gi·ªØa hai th√†nh ph·∫ßn.

<aside>
‚ö†Ô∏è

L∆∞u √Ω: c√¥ng th·ª©c tr√™n ch·ªâ d·∫°ng `abstract` v√¨ kh√≥ c√≥ th·ªÉ x√°c ƒë·ªãnh $L$ v√† $R$ tr·ª±c ti·∫øp tr√™n S

</aside>

Tr√™n th·ª±c t·∫ø, b√†i to√°n th·ªÉ hi·ªán hai c√°ch bi·ªÉu di·ªÖn: t∆∞·ªùng minh - **explicit** v√† ng·∫ßm ƒë·ªãnh - **implicit**

## **Explicit Representation**:

Surface $S$ ƒë∆∞·ª£c ƒë·ªãnh nghƒ©a qua m·ªôt h√†m `explicit representation` $f(x)$ trong kh√¥ng gian 3D:

$$
S = \{f(x) \in \mathbb{R}^3 \mid x \in \Omega^2\}
$$

- $\mathbbŒ©^2‚äÇ{R}^2$: mi·ªÅn tham s·ªë 2D.
- $f: \Omega^2 \to S$: H√†m √°nh x·∫° tham s·ªë t·ª´ kh√¥ng gian 2D $\Omega^2$ t·ªõi kh√¥ng gian 3D $S$

C√¥ng th·ª©c t·ªëi ∆∞u h√≥a t·ªïng qu√°t chuy·ªÉn th√†nh:

$$
\min_{f \in \mathcal{H}_f} \mathcal{L}_{\text{exp}}(f; P) + \lambda \mathcal{R}_{\text{exp}}(f)
$$

- $\mathcal{H}_f$: [**Hypothesis Space**](https://www.notion.so/Hypothesis-Space-1452a3f8f2a18068a3b8d0832f1956fb?pvs=21) ch·ª©a c√°c √°nh x·∫° $f$. V√≠ d·ª•, $f$ c√≥ th·ªÉ l√† c√°c ƒëa th·ª©c b·∫≠c th·∫•p, B-spline, ho·∫∑c c√°c m·∫°ng neural.
- $\mathcal{R}_{\text{exp}}(f)$: H√†m regularizer, gi√∫p ki·ªÉm so√°t ƒëi·ªÅu ki·ªán surface geometry $f(x)$.

H√†m explicit loss ƒë∆∞·ª£c vi·∫øt nh∆∞ sau:

$$
\mathcal{L}_{\text{exp}}(f; P) = \frac{1}{n_{p}} \sum_{p \in P} \min_{x \in \Omega^2} \|f(x) - p\|_l
$$

- $n_q$: s·ªë l∆∞·ª£ng point trong t·∫≠p $P$.
- $\|f(x) - p\|$: kho·∫£ng c√°ch Euclidean gi·ªØa ƒëi·ªÉm $f(x)$ tr√™n b·ªÅ m·∫∑t v√† ƒëi·ªÉm $p$ trong t·∫≠p d·ªØ li·ªáu.
- $\min_{x \in \Omega^2}:$ T√¨m ƒëi·ªÉm $f(x)$ g·∫ßn nh·∫•t v·ªõi $p$ trong kh√¥ng gian 3D.

**√ù nghƒ©a**: 

- V·ªõi m·ªói ƒëi·ªÉm $p \in P$ ƒë∆∞·ª£c ‚Äúkh·ªõp‚Äù v·ªõi √≠t nh·∫•t m·ªôt ƒëi·ªÉm $f(x)$ tr√™n b·ªÅ m·∫∑t $S$.

<aside>
‚ö†Ô∏è

Th·ª±c t·∫ø, vi·ªác t·ªëi ∆∞u tr√™n to√†n b·ªô mi·ªÅn $\Omega^2$ r·∫•t ph·ª©c t·∫°p, n√™n th∆∞·ªùng ch·ªâ l·∫•y m·ªôt t·∫≠p m·∫´u $\{x \in \Omega^2\}$
 d·ª±a tr√™n nhi·ªÅu bi·∫øn th·ªÉ `point-set distances` nh∆∞ Chamfer ho·∫∑c Hausdorff distances.

</aside>

## **Implicit Representation**:

Trong implicit representation, Surface $S$ ƒë∆∞·ª£c ƒë·ªãnh nghƒ©a l√† `zero-level set` c·ªßa m·ªôt h√†m implicit $F$:

$$
S = \{q \in \mathbb{R}^3 \mid F(q) = 0\}
$$

trong ƒë√≥ $F: \mathbb{R}^3 \to \mathbb{R}$ l√† h√†m implicit ƒë·ªãnh nghƒ©a b·ªÅ m·∫∑t $S$.

C√¥ng th·ª©c t·ªëi ∆∞u h√≥a t·ªïng qu√°t chuy·ªÉn th√†nh:

$$
\min_{F \in \mathcal{H}_F} \mathcal{L}_{\text{imp}}(F; P) + \lambda \mathcal{R}_{\text{imp}}(F)
$$

**Th√†nh ph·∫ßn**:

- $\mathcal{H}_F$: [**Hypothesis Space**](https://www.notion.so/Hypothesis-Space-1452a3f8f2a18068a3b8d0832f1956fb?pvs=21) ch·ª©a c√°c h√†m $F$, v√≠ d·ª•: m·∫°ng neural ho·∫∑c ƒëa th·ª©c.
- $\mathcal{R}_{\text{imp}}(f)$: Regularizer, gi√∫p ki·ªÉm so√°t ƒëi·ªÅu ki·ªán surface geometry $f(x)$.

H√†m loss implicit ƒë∆∞·ª£c vi·∫øt:

$$
\mathcal{L}_{\text{imp}}(F; P) = \frac{1}{n_P} \sum_{p \in P} \|F(p)\|_l
$$

- $F(p)$: gi√° tr·ªã c·ªßa h√†m $F$ t·∫°i ƒëi·ªÉm $p$. H√†m $F$ ƒë∆∞·ª£c thi·∫øt k·∫ø sao cho $F(p) = 0$  n·∫øu $p$ n·∫±m tr√™n b·ªÅ m·∫∑t, v√† $F(p) \neq 0$  n·∫øu $p$ c√°ch xa b·ªÅ m·∫∑t. **[**Signed Distance Function (SDF) & Occupancy Field**](https://www.notion.so/Signed-Distance-Function-SDF-Occupancy-Field-1442a3f8f2a18042b4a8f78a96230799?pvs=21)**
- $\|F(p)\|_l$: H√¨nh ph·∫°t n·∫øu ƒëi·ªÉm $p$ kh√¥ng th·ªèa m√£n. Th√¥ng th∆∞·ªùng $l = 1$ ho·∫∑c $l = 2$ .
- √ù nghƒ©a: C√¥ng th·ª©c n√†y gi√∫p "k√©o" c√°c ƒëi·ªÉm $p$ v√†o g·∫ßn b·ªÅ m·∫∑t $S$ b·∫±ng c√°ch gi·∫£m gi√° tr·ªã $F(p)$.

## **Advanced Implicit Losses**

B√†i b√°o c√≤n ƒë·ªÅ xu·∫•t m·ªü r·ªông h√†m implicit loss ƒë·ªÉ c·∫£i thi·ªán ch·∫•t l∆∞·ª£ng t√°i t·∫°o surface, s·ª≠ d·ª•ng c√¥ng th·ª©c:

$$
\mathcal{L}_{\text{imp++}}(F; P) = \alpha_1 \mathbb{E}_{q \in \mathbb{R}^3} \|F(q) - d(q; P)\|^2 + \alpha_2 \mathbb{E}_{q \in \mathbb{R}^3} \|\nabla_q F(q) - n(q; P)\|^2 + ...
$$

Gi·∫£i th√≠ch c√°c th√†nh ph·∫ßn:

1. $d(q; P)$: [**Signed Distance Function (SDF)**](https://www.notion.so/Surface-Reconstruction-From-Point-Clouds-A-Survey-and-a-Benchmark-1442a3f8f2a180aca990fd4b2793fb3b?pvs=21)
    - Kho·∫£ng c√°ch c√≥ d·∫•u gi·ªØa $q$ v√† b·ªÅ m·∫∑t $S$.
    - $d(q; P) = 0$ khi $q$ n·∫±m tr√™n b·ªÅ m·∫∑t, $d(q; P) > 0$ khi $q$ n·∫±m ngo√†i b·ªÅ m·∫∑t, v√† $d(q; P) < 0$ khi n·∫±m trong b·ªÅ m·∫∑t.
2. $\nabla_q F(q)$: [**Gradient**](https://www.notion.so/Surface-Reconstruction-From-Point-Clouds-A-Survey-and-a-Benchmark-1442a3f8f2a180aca990fd4b2793fb3b?pvs=21) c·ªßa $F$ t·∫°i $q$. 
    - Gradient n√†y ch·ªâ h∆∞·ªõng ph√°p tuy·∫øn `normal vector` c·ªßa surface t·∫°i $q$.
    - $n(q; P)$: Vector ph√°p tuy·∫øn th·ª±c t·∫ø t·∫°i ƒëi·ªÉm, ƒë∆∞·ª£c t√≠nh to√°n t·ª´ point cloud $P$.
3. Tr·ªçng s·ªë $\alpha_1, \alpha_2$: ƒëi·ªÅu ch·ªânh m·ª©c ƒë·ªô ∆∞u ti√™n gi·ªØa vi·ªác gi√° tr·ªã kho·∫£ng c√°ch v√† vector ph√°p tuy·∫øn.

**√ù nghƒ©a**:

- Th√†nh ph·∫ßn $\|F(q) - d(q; P)\|^2$: ƒê·∫£m b·∫£o $F(q)$ m√¥ h√¨nh h√≥a ch√≠nh x√°c **Signed Distance Function (SDF)**
- Th√†nh ph·∫ßn $\|\nabla_q F(q) - n(q; P)\|^2$: C·∫£i thi·ªán ƒë·ªô ch√≠nh x√°c c·ªßa b·ªÅ m·∫∑t v√† h∆∞·ªõng ph√°p tuy·∫øn.

![image.png](Surface%20Reconstruction%20From%20Point%20Clouds%20A%20Survey%20%201442a3f8f2a180aca990fd4b2793fb3b/image.png)

## **K·∫øt h·ª£p c√°c h√†m loss v√† regularization**

Do b√†i to√°n surface reconstruction l√† `ill-imposed`, ch·ªâ s·ª≠ d·ª•ng $\mathcal{L}(S; P)$ kh√¥ng ƒë·ªß ƒë·ªÉ t·∫°o ra m·ªôt surface h·ª£p l√Ω. V√¨ v·∫≠y, c·∫ßn th√™m **h√†m regularizer $\mathcal{R}(S)$** gi√∫p b√π ƒë·∫Øp h·∫°n ch·∫ø n√†y:

$$
\min_S \mathcal{L}(S; P) + \lambda \mathcal{R}(S)
$$

Regularizer $\mathcal{R}(S)$ ƒë∆∞·ª£c t√°c gi·∫£ nh√≥m d·ª±a tr√™n c√°c ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p nh∆∞ sau:

1. **Triangulation-based prior**
2. **Smoothness prior**
3. **Template-based prior**
4. **Modeling Prior**
5. **Learning-based Prior**
6. **Hybrid Prior**

**Details:**

- [**Explicit & Implicit**](https://www.notion.so/Explicit-Implicit-1442a3f8f2a180759082e4f386e812ad?pvs=21)
- [**Hypothesis Space**](https://www.notion.so/Hypothesis-Space-1452a3f8f2a18068a3b8d0832f1956fb?pvs=21)
- [**Data Fidelity**](https://www.notion.so/Data-Fidelity-1442a3f8f2a180bcbfdef563f8d1ceb7?pvs=21)

- [**Local Tangent Plane, Normal Vector** ](https://www.notion.so/Local-Tangent-Plane-Normal-Vector-1442a3f8f2a180e9a485de88b59e4fdf?pvs=21)
- [**Gradient**](https://www.notion.so/Gradient-1452a3f8f2a18094954cd5a95913f7ee?pvs=21)

# Surface Reconstruction with a Categorization of Geometric Priors

## Triangulation-Based Prior

![image.png](Surface%20Reconstruction%20From%20Point%20Clouds%20A%20Survey%20%201442a3f8f2a180aca990fd4b2793fb3b/image%201.png)

![image.png](Surface%20Reconstruction%20From%20Point%20Clouds%20A%20Survey%20%201442a3f8f2a180aca990fd4b2793fb3b/image%202.png)

[Simple Stereo | Camera Calibration](https://youtu.be/hUVyDabn1Mg?si=qcnRsHgYDfZ4emO4)

Triangulation using Two Cameras

**Triangulation-based prior** l√† m·ªôt ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p classical trong b√†i to√°n *surface reconstruction*. Ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p t·∫≠n d·ª•ng gi·∫£ thi·∫øt r·∫±ng b·ªÅ m·∫∑t $S$ c√≥ th·ªÉ ƒë∆∞·ª£c bi·ªÉu di·ªÖn b·∫±ng m·ªôt **l∆∞·ªõi tam gi√°c (triangular mesh)**, ƒë·∫∑c bi·ªát hi·ªáu qu·∫£ khi b·ªÅ m·∫∑t $S$ c√≥ t√≠nh ch·∫•t tr∆°n c·ª•c b·ªô *[**Locally Differentiable**](https://www.notion.so/Locally-Differentiable-1462a3f8f2a18068a642ee6ffb807c5f?pvs=21)  [**Piecewise Linear**](https://www.notion.so/Piecewise-Linear-1462a3f8f2a180fab89dcbfae3d448da?pvs=21) .* Ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p n√†y th∆∞·ªùng √°p d·ª•ng thu·∫≠t to√°n **Delaunay triangulation**, v·ªõi c√°c b∆∞·ªõc v√† c√¥ng th·ª©c to√°n h·ªçc c·ª• th·ªÉ nh∆∞ sau:

<aside>
üí°

A closed surface is continuous and could be locally differentiable up to different orders

</aside>

- N·∫øu $S$ `kh·∫£ vi b·∫≠c nh·∫•t` [**Locally Differentiable up to First Order**](https://www.notion.so/Locally-Differentiable-up-to-First-Order-1462a3f8f2a1809caedbdb095899ba6c?pvs=21), th√¨ ta c√≥ th·ªÉ x·∫•p x·ªâ $S$
  b·∫±ng m·ªôt t·∫≠p h·ª£p c√°c **tam gi√°c ph·∫≥ng (flat triangles)** ƒë∆∞·ª£c gh√©p l·∫°i. ƒêi·ªÅu n√†y cho ph√©p m√¥ h√¨nh h√≥a b·ªÅ m·∫∑t b·∫±ng m·ªôt **l∆∞·ªõi tam gi√°c (triangular mesh)**.
- **Bi·ªÉu di·ªÖn l∆∞·ªõi tam gi√°c**: M·ªôt l∆∞·ªõi tam gi√°c $G_S$ g·ªìm c√°c tam gi√°c $\{T_i\}_{i=1}^{n_G}$, trong ƒë√≥ m·ªói tam gi√°c $T$ ƒë∆∞·ª£c x√°c ƒë·ªãnh b·ªüi ba ƒë·ªânh $\{v_1^T, v_2^T, v_3^T\} \subset P$.

**Delaunay triangulation** l√† m·ªôt ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p triangular mesh ph·ªï bi·∫øn, v·ªõi ƒëi·ªÅu ki·ªán:

1. **Empty Sphere Property**: Kh√¥ng c√≥ ƒëi·ªÉm n√†o trong t·∫≠p $P$ n·∫±m b√™n trong m·∫∑t c·∫ßu ngo·∫°i ti·∫øp $\text{CC}(T)$ tam gi√°c $T$.
2. **T√≠nh ch·∫•t h√¨nh h·ªçc t·ªët**: Tam gi√°c ƒë∆∞·ª£c t·∫°o ra c√≥ g√≥c nh·ªçn l·ªõn nh·∫•t c√≥ th·ªÉ, gi√∫p gi·∫£m thi·ªÉu c√°c tam gi√°c "x·∫•u" (nh∆∞ tam gi√°c d·∫πt ho·∫∑c kh√¥ng ƒë·ªÅu).

![image.png](Surface%20Reconstruction%20From%20Point%20Clouds%20A%20Survey%20%201442a3f8f2a180aca990fd4b2793fb3b/image%203.png)

[Delaunay Triangulation](https://youtu.be/GctAunEuHt4?si=9eP0ZMIORa1MxxeE)

[Delaunay Triangulation](https://gwlucastrig.github.io/TinfourDocs/DelaunayIntro/index.html)

**Triangular mesh** $G_S$ ƒë∆∞·ª£c x√¢y d·ª±ng th·ªèa m√£n:

$$
G_S = \{T_i\}_{i=1}^{n_G}, \quad \text{v·ªõi } v_1^T, v_2^T, v_3^T \in P, \forall T \in G_S
$$

$$
p \notin \text{CC}(T), \forall p \in P \setminus \{v_1^T, v_2^T, v_3^T\}, \forall T \in G_S
$$

Trong ƒë√≥:

- $T = \{v_1^T, v_2^T, v_3^T\}$: M·ªôt tam gi√°c ph·∫≥ng ƒë∆∞·ª£c ƒë·ªãnh nghƒ©a b·ªüi ba ƒëi·ªÉm $v_1^T, v_2^T, v_3^T$.
- $\text{CC}(T)$: Kh√¥ng gian b√™n trong m·∫∑t c·∫ßu ngo·∫°i ti·∫øp *[**Circumscribing Sphere of a Triangle**](https://www.notion.so/Circumscribing-Sphere-of-a-Triangle-1462a3f8f2a1801caa51c3fd3bcaf7a0?pvs=21)*  c·ªßa tam gi√°c $T$.
- **ƒêi·ªÅu ki·ªán**: Kh√¥ng c√≥ ƒëi·ªÉm n√†o kh√°c trong $P$ n·∫±m b√™n trong $CC(T)$.

**√ù nghƒ©a c·ªßa c√¥ng th·ª©c**:

- **Empty Sphere Property**: B·∫£o ƒë·∫£m l∆∞·ªõi tam gi√°c ƒë∆∞·ª£c t·ªëi ∆∞u v·ªÅ h√¨nh h·ªçc, gi·∫£m thi·ªÉu tam gi√°c d·∫πt v√† t·ªëi ƒëa h√≥a smooth c·ªßa b·ªÅ m·∫∑t.
- **ƒê·∫∑c ƒëi·ªÉm ph√π h·ª£p v·ªõi d·ªØ li·ªáu**: T·∫•t c·∫£ c√°c tam gi√°c ƒë∆∞·ª£c t·∫°o ra ƒë·ªÅu c√≥ ƒë·ªânh thu·ªôc t·∫≠p $P$, b·∫£o ƒë·∫£m reconstruct surface g·∫ßn v·ªõi observed $P$.

**∆Øu ƒëi·ªÉm**:

- Ph√π h·ª£p cho c√°c b·ªÅ m·∫∑t ƒë∆°n gi·∫£n.
- Cung c·∫•p c·∫•u tr√∫c l∆∞·ªõi c√≥ t√≠nh ch·∫•t h√¨nh h·ªçc t·ªët.
- Linh ho·∫°t v·ªõi c√°c h√¨nh d·∫°ng ph·ª©c t·∫°p trong kh√¥ng gian 2D.

**Nh∆∞·ª£c ƒëi·ªÉm**:

- **Kh√¥ng ƒë·ªãnh nghƒ©a t·ªët trong kh√¥ng gian 3D**: Khi √°p d·ª•ng v√†o kh√¥ng gian 3D, c√°c tam gi√°c c√≥ th·ªÉ kh√¥ng duy tr√¨ ƒë∆∞·ª£c t√≠nh ch·∫•t h√¨nh h·ªçc t·ªët.
- H·∫ßu h·∫øt ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p t√°i t·∫°o s·ª≠ d·ª•ng ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p n√†y nh∆∞ `initialization` , `regularization` , ho·∫∑c m·ªü r·ªông th√†nh `Delaunay Terhedarization`
    
    <aside>
    üí°
    
    Most reconstruction methods take it as an initialization [41] or regularization [42], or extend Delaunay tetrahedralization to remove the triangles of undesirable shape in reconstruction [6].
    
    </aside>
    

**C√°c ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p c·ª• th·ªÉ s·ª≠ d·ª•ng Triangulation-Based Prior**

1. **Greedy Delaunay (GD)**
    - S·ª≠ d·ª•ng greedy algorithm ƒë·ªÉ ch·ªçn tam gi√°c kh·∫£ thi d·ª±a tr√™n c√°c r√†ng bu·ªôc t√¥-p√¥ *[**Topological Constraints** ](https://www.notion.so/Topological-Constraints-1462a3f8f2a180749d6beda19d4cccd5?pvs=21)*
    
    [What is a Greedy Algorithm? Examples of Greedy Algorithms](https://www.freecodecamp.org/news/greedy-algorithms/)
    
    - C√°c b∆∞·ªõc ch√≠nh:
        1. T·∫°o t·∫≠p h·ª£p c√°c tam gi√°c ban ƒë·∫ßu t·ª´ Delaunay triangulation.
        2. Ch·ªçn d·∫ßn c√°c tam gi√°c tho·∫£ m√£n ƒëi·ªÅu ki·ªán h√¨nh h·ªçc v√† t√¥-p√¥.
2. **Ball-Pivoting Algorithm (BPA)**
    
    ![image.png](Surface%20Reconstruction%20From%20Point%20Clouds%20A%20Survey%20%201442a3f8f2a180aca990fd4b2793fb3b/image%204.png)
    
    [The Ball Pivoting Algorithm -  ppt video online download](https://slideplayer.com/slide/4773919/)
    
    - Ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p t·∫°o tam gi√°c b·∫±ng c√°ch s·ª≠ d·ª•ng **qu·∫£ c·∫ßu lƒÉn (rolling ball)**:
        - M·ªôt qu·∫£ c·∫ßu c√≥ b√°n k√≠nh $r$ x√°c ƒë·ªãnh lƒÉn qua c√°c ƒëi·ªÉm trong $P$.
        - Ba ƒëi·ªÉm $\{p_1, p_2, p_3\}$ ƒë∆∞·ª£c ch·ªçn t·∫°o th√†nh tam gi√°c n·∫øu qu·∫£ c·∫ßu ti·∫øp x√∫c ƒë·ªìng th·ªùi c·∫£ ba ƒëi·ªÉm m√† kh√¥ng ch·ª©a ƒëi·ªÉm n√†o kh√°c b√™n trong.
    - **∆Øu ƒëi·ªÉm**: BPA g·∫ßn gi·ªëng v·ªõi Delaunay nh∆∞ng linh ho·∫°t h∆°n trong kh√¥ng gian 3D.

## Surface Smoothness Priors

![image.png](Surface%20Reconstruction%20From%20Point%20Clouds%20A%20Survey%20%201442a3f8f2a180aca990fd4b2793fb3b/image%205.png)

![image.png](Surface%20Reconstruction%20From%20Point%20Clouds%20A%20Survey%20%201442a3f8f2a180aca990fd4b2793fb3b/image%206.png)

Trong b√†i to√°n surface reconstruction, b·ªÅ m·∫∑t $S$ c·∫ßn ƒë∆∞·ª£c [`smooth`](https://www.notion.so/Surface-Reconstruction-From-Point-Clouds-A-Survey-and-a-Benchmark-1442a3f8f2a180aca990fd4b2793fb3b?pvs=21) ho·∫∑c √≠t nh·∫•t l√† `continuosly differentiable` m·ªôt m·ª©c ƒë·ªô n√†o ƒë√≥. ƒêi·ªÅu n√†y gi√∫p:

- **Gi·∫£m nhi·ªÖu (noise)**: Lo·∫°i b·ªè c√°c dao ƒë·ªông nh·ªè ho·∫∑c b·∫•t th∆∞·ªùng trong d·ªØ li·ªáu.
- **T·∫°o h√¨nh d·∫°ng t·ª± nhi√™n h∆°n**: ƒê·∫£m b·∫£o b·ªÅ m·∫∑t kh√¥ng b·ªã g·ªì gh·ªÅ ho·∫∑c kh√¥ng th·ª±c t·∫ø.

C√≥ ba strategies ƒë·ªÉ √°p ƒë·∫∑t r√†ng bu·ªôc [smooth](https://www.notion.so/Surface-Reconstruction-From-Point-Clouds-A-Survey-and-a-Benchmark-1442a3f8f2a180aca990fd4b2793fb3b?pvs=21):

1. [**Surface Smoothness via Local Weighted Combination**](https://www.notion.so/Surface-Reconstruction-From-Point-Clouds-A-Survey-and-a-Benchmark-1442a3f8f2a180aca990fd4b2793fb3b?pvs=21)
2. [**Surface smoothness by combination of strategies**](https://www.notion.so/Surface-Reconstruction-From-Point-Clouds-A-Survey-and-a-Benchmark-1442a3f8f2a180aca990fd4b2793fb3b?pvs=21)
3. [**Surface smoothness by constraining function complexities**](https://www.notion.so/Surface-Reconstruction-From-Point-Clouds-A-Survey-and-a-Benchmark-1442a3f8f2a180aca990fd4b2793fb3b?pvs=21)

### **Local Weighted Combination**

Chi·∫øn l∆∞·ª£c n√†y d·ª±a tr√™n √Ω t∆∞·ªüng r·∫±ng m·ªói ƒëi·ªÉm $p$ trong point cloud s·∫Ω ƒë∆∞·ª£c ƒëi·ªÅu ch·ªânh d·ª±a tr√™n c√°c ƒëi·ªÉm `local neighborhood` c·ªßa $p$.

$$
\min_{f} \mathcal{L}_{\text{exp}}(f; P) = \frac{1}{n_P} \sum_{p \in P} \min_{x \in \Omega^2} \|f(x) - \hat{p}(p)\|^2
$$

**Gi·∫£i th√≠ch c√°c th√†nh ph·∫ßn:**

- $n_P$: S·ªë ƒëi·ªÉm trong t·∫≠p $P$ (ƒë·ªô l·ªõn c·ªßa d·ªØ li·ªáu).
- $f(x)$: H√†m √°nh x·∫° t·ª´ mi·ªÅn tham s·ªë $\Omega^2 \subset \mathbb{R}^2$ƒë·∫øn kh√¥ng gian 3D, bi·ªÉu di·ªÖn b·ªÅ m·∫∑t $S$.
- $\hat{p}(p)$: ƒêi·ªÉm ƒë∆∞·ª£c l√†m smooth c·ªßa $p$, t√≠nh d·ª±a tr√™n c√°c ƒëi·ªÉm l√¢n c·∫≠n $N(p)$.

**C√°ch t√≠nh $\hat{p}(p)$**:

$$
\hat{p}(p) = \sum_{p' \in N(p)} p' g(\|p - p'\|)
$$

**Gi·∫£i th√≠ch:**

- $N(p)$: `local neighborhood` c·ªßa ƒëi·ªÉm $p$, t·ª©c l√† t·∫≠p h·ª£p c√°c ƒëi·ªÉm g·∫ßn $p$ trong kh√¥ng gian 3D.
- $g(\|p - p'\|)$: H√†m tr·ªçng s·ªë, gi·∫£m gi√° tr·ªã khi kho·∫£ng c√°ch $\|p - p'\|$ tƒÉng. M·ªôt v√≠ d·ª• ph·ªï bi·∫øn l√† [Radial Basis Function (RBF)](https://www.notion.so/Radial-Basis-Function-RBF-1462a3f8f2a180958de9e2e8325d6b64?pvs=21) :
    
    $$
    g(r) = \exp\left(-\frac{r^2}{2\sigma^2}\right)
    $$
    
    - $\sigma$: ƒêi·ªÅu ch·ªânh ph·∫°m vi ·∫£nh h∆∞·ªüng c·ªßa kho·∫£ng c√°ch.

H√£y t∆∞·ªüng t∆∞·ª£ng b·∫°n c√≥ m·ªôt t·∫≠p ƒëi·ªÉm 3D, trong ƒë√≥ m·ªôt s·ªë ƒëi·ªÉm b·ªã noise v√† kh√¥ng n·∫±m ƒë√∫ng tr√™n b·ªÅ m·∫∑t $S$ th·ª±c s·ª±. ƒê·ªÉ l√†m b·ªÅ m·∫∑t smooth, b·∫°n s·∫Ω:

1. X√°c ƒë·ªãnh c√°c ƒëi·ªÉm neighbor c·ªßa m·ªói ƒëi·ªÉm $p$ (b·∫±ng c√°ch ch·ªçn c√°c ƒëi·ªÉm trong b√°n k√≠nh nh·∫•t ƒë·ªãnh, v√≠ d·ª• $r = 0.1$).
2. T√≠nh trung b√¨nh c√≥ tr·ªçng s·ªë c·ªßa c√°c ƒëi·ªÉm neighbor d·ª±a tr√™n kho·∫£ng c√°ch c·ªßa ch√∫ng ƒë·∫øn $p$.
3. S·ª≠ d·ª•ng gi√° tr·ªã n√†y ƒë·ªÉ thay th·∫ø $p$, l√†m `smooth` n√≥.

**Poisson Surface Reconstruction (PSR)** l√† m·ªôt ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p l√†m smooth b·ªÅ m·∫∑t t∆∞∆°ng t·ª±, √°p d·ª•ng trong tr∆∞·ªùng h·ª£p s·ª≠ d·ª•ng implicit representation b·∫±ng regularize smooth th√¥ng qua gradient c·ªßa tr∆∞·ªùng vector ph√°p tuy·∫øn:

$$
\mathcal{L}_{\text{PSR}}(F; P) = \mathbb{E}_{q \in \mathbb{R}^3} \|\nabla_q F(q) - \hat{n}(q; P)\|^2
$$

- $F(q)$: H√†m implicit b·ªÅ m·∫∑t $S$ th√¥ng qua `zero-level set` $S = \{q \in \mathbb{R}^3 | F(q) = 0\}$
- $\nabla_q F(q)$: Gradient c·ªßa $F$, th·ªÉ hi·ªán h∆∞·ªõng ph√°p tuy·∫øn `normal vector` c·ªßa b·ªÅ m·∫∑t $S$ t·∫°i ƒëi·ªÉm $q$.
- $\hat{n}(q; P)$: Tr∆∞·ªùng ph√°p tuy·∫øn `normal` trung b√¨nh t·∫°i q, ƒë∆∞·ª£c t√≠nh t·ª´ c√°c ƒëi·ªÉm neighbor $N(q)$:

$$
\hat{n}(q; P) = \sum_{p' \in N(q)} n(p'; P) g(\|q - p'\|)
$$

- $n(p^{'}; P)$: Ph√°p tuy·∫øn t·∫°i ƒëi·ªÉm $p'$, th∆∞·ªùng ƒë∆∞·ª£c t√≠nh th√¥ng qua PCA t·ª´ neighbours.

**√ù nghƒ©a**: PSR c·ªë g·∫Øng kh·ªõp gradient c·ªßa $F(q)$ v·ªõi local normal $\hat{n}(q; P)$, gi√∫p b·ªÅ m·∫∑t $S$ smooth h∆°n.

V·∫•n ƒë·ªÅ PSR th∆∞·ªùng t·∫°o ra b·ªÅ m·∫∑t qu√° smooth v√† m·∫•t ƒëi c√°c chi ti·∫øt details. **Screened Poisson Surface Reconstruction** (**SPSR)** kh·∫Øc ph·ª•c nh∆∞·ª£c ƒëi·ªÉm n√†y b·∫±ng c√°ch k·∫øt h·ª£p ƒëi·ªÅu ch·ªânh c·∫£ c√°c regularizer b·∫≠c m·ªôt v√† b·∫≠c hai trong h√†m loss advanced implicit

<aside>
üí°

As a remedy, Screened Poisson Surface Reconstruction (SPSR) [39] improves over PSR by incorporating regularized versions of both the first- and second-order terms in (7).

</aside>

G·∫ßn ƒë√¢y, https://pengsongyou.github.io/sap ra ƒë·ªùi `is more interpretable, lightweight, and accelerates inference time by one order of magnitude.` End-to-end optimization, v√† c√≥ th·ªÉ integrate deep neural networks. 

<aside>
üí°

Shape As Points [44] develops a differentiable Poisson solver in a spectral manner, which enables an end-to-end optimization and thus could be integrated into the learning of deep neural networks.

</aside>

### Constraining function complexities

B·∫±ng c√°ch gi·ªõi h·∫°n [**Hypothesis Space**](https://www.notion.so/Hypothesis-Space-1452a3f8f2a18068a3b8d0832f1956fb?pvs=21) $H_f$ ho·∫∑c $H_{F}$ nh∆∞ `B-spline functions`, `NURBS`, `Gaussians` ƒë·ªÉ tr√°nh hi·ªán t∆∞·ª£ng `overfiiting` - l√†m b·ªÅ m·∫∑t √≠t smooth h∆°n.

V√≠ d·ª•:

1. S·ª≠ d·ª•ng h√†m c∆° b·∫£n [Gaussian (RBF)](https://www.notion.so/Surface-Reconstruction-From-Point-Clouds-A-Survey-and-a-Benchmark-1442a3f8f2a180aca990fd4b2793fb3b?pvs=21) [53] :  √Åp d·ª•ng c√°c ƒëa th·ª©c b·∫≠c th·∫•p ƒë·ªÉ x·∫•p x·ªâ implicit ho·∫∑c explicit function.
2. **Fourier Transform [54]**: s·ª≠ d·ª•ng c√°c h·ªá s·ªë Fourier ƒë·ªÉ bi·ªÉu di·ªÖn b·ªÅ m·∫∑t v√† t√°i t·∫°o b·∫±ng c√°ch s·ª≠ d·ª•ng **Divergence Theorem** https://youtu.be/vZGvgru4TwE?si=kpYY1cXCvvJXb-pS.
3. **Wavelet Representation [55]**: s·ª≠ d·ª•ng wavelets ƒë·ªÉ cung c·∫•p m√¥ h√¨nh ƒëa ƒë·ªô ph√¢n gi·∫£i (multi-resolution) nh·∫±m c·∫£i thi·ªán chi ti·∫øt.
4. Instead of using a regular grid, [50] optimizes the likelihood function over a finer grid under some topological constraints by solving the parameters of the Gaussian basis function.
5. He et al. [56] propose to regularize the curvatures of the mesh when reconstructing the surface, which results in a reconstructed surface that is smoother.
6. Wang [51] introduces a **Gaussian convolution** to the energy term, which promotes smoothness on the learned implicit function during the iterative optimization process.
7. **PGR** [52] chooses the basis of the indicator function that is guided by a Gaussian formulation to recover the surface from un-oriented points.

### Combination of Strategies

Chi·∫øn l∆∞·ª£c k·∫øt h·ª£p (combination of strategies) trong vi·ªác ƒë·∫£m b·∫£o smooth c·ªßa b·ªÅ m·∫∑t d·ª±a tr√™n s·ª± t√≠ch h·ª£p c√°c ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p ƒë√£ ƒë∆∞·ª£c ƒë·ªÅ c·∫≠p, c·ª• th·ªÉ l√†:

1. K·∫øt h·ª£p tr·ªçng s·ªë c·ª•c b·ªô (Local Weighted Combination).
2. Gi·ªõi h·∫°n ƒë·ªô ph·ª©c t·∫°p h√†m (Constrained Function Complexities).

[www.cs.jhu.edu](https://www.cs.jhu.edu/~misha/Fall05/Papers/alexa01.pdf)

Point Set Surfaces Paper

C√°c ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p nh∆∞ **Point Set Surfaces (PSS)** t·∫≠n d·ª•ng s·ª©c m·∫°nh c·ªßa c·∫£ hai strategies tr√™n, t·∫°o ra b·ªÅ m·∫∑t smooth t·ª´ t·∫≠p h·ª£p c√°c ƒëi·ªÉm observed $P$. PSS xu·∫•t ph√°t t·ª´ l√Ω thuy·∫øt **Moving Least Squares (MLS)**, l√† m·ªôt k·ªπ thu·∫≠t quan tr·ªçng trong vi·ªác x√¢y d·ª±ng b·ªÅ m·∫∑t t·ª´ ƒë√°m m√¢y ƒëi·ªÉm. MLS c√≥ th·ªÉ ƒë∆∞·ª£c s·ª≠ d·ª•ng ƒë·ªÉ ƒë·ªãnh nghƒ©a b·ªÅ m·∫∑t theo:

1. **H√†m t∆∞·ªùng minh (explicit function)**: X√¢y d·ª±ng b·ªÅ m·∫∑t qua c√°c ph√©p chi·∫øu (project) tr·ª±c ti·∫øp l√™n kh√¥ng gian tham s·ªë.
2. **H√†m ng·∫ßm (implicit function)**: ƒê·∫°i di·ªán b·ªÅ m·∫∑t th√¥ng qua c√°c gi√° tr·ªã m·∫∑t m·ª©c (level set).

PSS s·ª≠ d·ª•ng **k·∫øt h·ª£p tr·ªçng s·ªë c·ª•c b·ªô c·ªßa c√°c ƒëa th·ª©c b·∫≠c th·∫•p (spatially-varying low-degree polynomials)** ƒë·ªÉ:

- X·∫•p x·ªâ c√°c ƒëi·ªÉm quan s√°t $P$ trong m·ªôt local neighbor.
- X√¢y d·ª±ng b·ªÅ m·∫∑t b·∫±ng c√°ch t·ªëi ∆∞u h√≥a c√°c ƒëa th·ª©c n√†y c·ª•c b·ªô t·∫°i m·ªói ƒëi·ªÉm.

‚Üí C√°c ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p nh∆∞ **SPSS, Algebraic PSS**, v√† **RIMLS** c·∫£i thi·ªán hi·ªáu su·∫•t, m·ªü r·ªông kh·∫£ nƒÉng t√°i t·∫°o b·ªÅ m·∫∑t trong c√°c t√¨nh hu·ªëng ph·ª©c t·∫°p h∆°n.

‚Üí C√°ch ti·∫øp c·∫≠n th√¥ng qua **Moving Least Squares (MLS)** v·∫´n gi·ªØ vai tr√≤ n·ªÅn t·∫£ng, k·∫øt h·ª£p v·ªõi c√°c thu·∫≠t to√°n c·∫£i ti·∫øn ƒë·ªÉ ƒë·∫°t ƒë∆∞·ª£c ƒë·ªô ch√≠nh x√°c cao h∆°n.

[Moving least squares](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Moving_least_squares)

## Template-Based Priors

![image.png](Surface%20Reconstruction%20From%20Point%20Clouds%20A%20Survey%20%201442a3f8f2a180aca990fd4b2793fb3b/image%207.png)

**Template-based priors** gi·∫£ ƒë·ªãnh r·∫±ng b·ªÅ m·∫∑t c·∫ßn t√°i t·∫°o c√≥ th·ªÉ ƒë∆∞·ª£c bi·ªÉu di·ªÖn b·∫±ng c√°ch **k·∫øt h·ª£p m·ªôt nh√≥m c√°c templates**. C√°c templates n√†y c√≥ th·ªÉ l√†:

- **Geometric primitives (h√¨nh h·ªçc c∆° b·∫£n)**: H√¨nh c·∫ßu, h√¨nh h·ªôp, h√¨nh tr·ª•, h√¨nh n√≥n, v.v.
- **Complex templates (m·∫´u ph·ª©c t·∫°p)**: ƒê∆∞·ª£c l·∫•y t·ª´ m·ªôt t·∫≠p d·ªØ li·ªáu ph·ª• tr·ª£ (auxiliary dataset).

Qu√° tr√¨nh surface reconstruction ƒë∆∞·ª£c `boil downs` th√†nh b√†i to√°n:

1. T√¨m c√°c m·∫´u ph√π h·ª£p t·ª´ t·∫≠p templates ƒë√£ cho.
2. Estimating/ fitting correct templates sao cho kh·ªõp v·ªõi observed $P$.

B√†i to√°n ƒë∆∞·ª£c ƒë·ªãnh nghƒ©a d∆∞·ªõi d·∫°ng:

$$
\min_{\{w\}, \{\theta\}} D\left( \sum_{i=1}^{|M|} w_i M_i(\theta_i), P \right)
$$

Trong ƒë√≥:

- $\{M\} = \{M_1, M_2, \dots, M_{|M|}\}$: T·∫≠p h·ª£p c√°c templates ƒë√£ ƒë∆∞·ª£c ƒë·ªãnh nghƒ©a tr∆∞·ªõc.
- $w_i$: Tr·ªçng s·ªë cho m·ªói template $M_i$. Tr·ªçng s·ªë n√†y c√≥ th·ªÉ l√† bi·∫øn s·ªë c·∫ßn optimize ho·∫∑c ƒë√£ ƒë∆∞·ª£c c·ªë ƒë·ªãnh.
- $M_i(\theta_i)$: M·ªói template $M_i$ ƒë∆∞·ª£c tham s·ªë h√≥a b·ªüi $\theta_i$, c√°c tham s·ªë n√†y c√≥ th·ªÉ ƒë∆∞·ª£c h·ªçc `learnable parameters`.
- $D(\cdot, \cdot)$: H√†m kho·∫£ng c√°ch ƒëo s·ª± kh√°c bi·ªát gi·ªØa b·ªÅ m·∫∑t ƒë∆∞·ª£c t√°i t·∫°o $\sum_{i} w_i M_i(\theta_i)$ v√† t·∫≠p ƒëi·ªÉm quan s√°t $P$. V√≠ d·ª•: $D$ c√≥ th·ªÉ l√† t·ªïng b√¨nh ph∆∞∆°ng kho·∫£ng c√°ch Euclidean

**√ù nghƒ©a**: Khi minimize h√†m $D$, ta t√¨m ƒë∆∞·ª£c t·∫≠p tr·ªçng s·ªë $\{w\}$ v√† tham s·ªë $\{\theta\}$ ƒë·ªÉ b·ªÅ m·∫∑t t·∫°o th√†nh t·ª´ templates g·∫ßn kh·ªõp nh·∫•t v·ªõi t·∫≠p ƒëi·ªÉm observed $P$.

**C√°c sub-methods c·ª• th·ªÉ bao g·ªìm:**

### **1. Geometric Primitives**

Templates ƒë∆°n gi·∫£n bao g·ªìm c√°c h√¨nh h·ªçc c∆° b·∫£n nh∆∞: **Cuboids (h√¨nh h·ªôp)**, **spheres (h√¨nh c·∫ßu)**, **cylinders (h√¨nh tr·ª•)**, **cones (h√¨nh n√≥n)**, v.v. C√°c h√¨nh h·ªçc n√†y c√≥ th·ªÉ ƒë∆∞·ª£c bi·ªÉu di·ªÖn ch√≠nh x√°c b·∫±ng m·ªôt s·ªë √≠t tham s·ªë (v√≠ d·ª•: b√°n k√≠nh c·ªßa h√¨nh c·∫ßu, chi·ªÅu cao v√† b√°n k√≠nh c·ªßa h√¨nh tr·ª•).

**Gi·∫£i thu·∫≠t: Random Sample Consensus (RANSAC)**

[Dealing with Outliers: RANSAC | Image Stitching](https://youtu.be/EkYXjmiolBg?si=wNcAeIT3NDyILxEJ)

RANSAC l√† ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p ph·ªï bi·∫øn ƒë·ªÉ gi·∫£i b√†i to√°n $\min D(\cdot, P)$ v·ªõi c√°c templates h√¨nh h·ªçc c∆° b·∫£n:

1. **√ù t∆∞·ªüng**:
    - RANSAC l·∫∑p l·∫°i qu√° tr√¨nh ch·ªçn ng·∫´u nhi√™n c√°c ƒëi·ªÉm $p$ t·ª´ t·∫≠p $P$ ƒë·ªÉ kh·ªõp v·ªõi m·ªôt m·∫´u $M_i$.
    - T√≠nh to√°n ƒëi·ªÉm s·ªë (score) d·ª±a tr√™n m·ª©c ƒë·ªô ‚Äúkh·ªõp‚Äù c·ªßa m·∫´u $M_i$ v·ªõi d·ªØ li·ªáu quan s√°t.
    - L·ª±a ch·ªçn m·∫´u c√≥ ƒëi·ªÉm s·ªë cao nh·∫•t.
2. **V√≠ d·ª• trong nghi√™n c·ª©u**:
    - **Schnabel et al. [65]**: ƒê·ªÅ xu·∫•t thu·∫≠t to√°n RANSAC hi·ªáu qu·∫£ v·ªõi chi·∫øn l∆∞·ª£c ch·ªçn m·∫´u th√¥ng minh v√† ƒë√°nh gi√° ƒëi·ªÉm s·ªë nhanh ch√≥ng.
    
    <aside>
    üí°
    
    Schnabel et al. [65] introduce an efficient RANSAC-based algorithm with a novel sampling strategy and an efficient score evaluation scheme, where the primitive with maximum score is extracted iteratively.
    
    </aside>
    
    - **Nan v√† Wonka [66]**: Ch·ªâ t·∫≠p trung tr√≠ch xu·∫•t c√°c m·∫´u ph·∫≥ng (planar primitives) t·ª´ RANSAC v√† t·ªëi ∆∞u h√≥a t·ªïng h·ª£p b·ªÅ m·∫∑t b·∫±ng c√°ch s·ª≠ d·ª•ng tr·ªçng s·ªë nƒÉng l∆∞·ª£ng (weighted sum of energy terms).
    
    <aside>
    üí°
    
    Nan and Wonka [66] propose to only extract planar primitives based on RANSAC, obtaining the final surface by minimizing a weighted sum of several energy terms to select the optimal set of faces.
    
    </aside>
    
3. **·ª®ng d·ª•ng kh√°c**: **Zhu et al. [67]**: S·ª≠ d·ª•ng c√°c patch (m·∫£nh nh·ªè) t·ª´ point cloud v√† √°p d·ª•ng c√°c ph∆∞∆°ng tr√¨nh ƒë·∫°o h√†m ri√™ng (partial differential equations) ƒë·ªÉ t√°i t·∫°o b·ªÅ m·∫∑t t·ª´ c√°c templates kh√°c nhau.
    
    <aside>
    üí°
    
    Zhu et al. [67] reconstruct the surface by fitting the segmented point clouds with different primitive patches defined by the solution of the partial differentiable equation.
    
    </aside>
    

**∆Øu ƒëi·ªÉm**: Ph√π h·ª£p v·ªõi c√°c b·ªÅ m·∫∑t c√≥ c·∫•u tr√∫c ƒë∆°n gi·∫£n ho·∫∑c c√°c v·∫≠t th·ªÉ ƒë∆∞·ª£c m√¥ h√¨nh h√≥a b·∫±ng c√°c h√¨nh h·ªçc c∆° b·∫£n.

### 2. Retrieval-Based Templates

Ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p n√†y s·ª≠ d·ª•ng m·ªôt t·∫≠p template ph·ª• tr·ª£ `auxiliary set` $\{M\}$, th∆∞·ªùng l√† c√°c m√¥ h√¨nh ph·ª©c t·∫°p ƒë∆∞·ª£c l∆∞u tr·ªØ tr∆∞·ªõc (auxiliary dataset), ƒë·ªÉ:

1. T√¨m ki·∫øm `retrieve` c√°c template g·∫ßn ƒë√∫ng nh·∫•t.
2. Bi·∫øn d·∫°ng `deform` c√°c template n√†y ƒë·ªÉ kh·ªõp v·ªõi t·∫≠p ƒëi·ªÉm $P$.

**C√°ch th·ª©c ho·∫°t ƒë·ªông**:

- **Scene Reconstruction**:
    - Point cloud $P$¬†ƒë∆∞·ª£c segmented th√†nh c√°c `semantic classes`.
    - M·ªói class ƒë∆∞·ª£c kh·ªõp v·ªõi m·ªôt template ƒë√£ l∆∞u `retrieved template`, sau ƒë√≥ ƒëi·ªÅu ch·ªânh b·∫±ng c√°c ph√©p `rigid` ho·∫∑c `non-rigid deformation`.

[www.uoanbar.edu.iq](https://www.uoanbar.edu.iq/eStoreImages/Bank/7116.pdf)

rigid and non-rigid deformation

- **Object Reconstruction**:
    - **Pauly et al. [72]**: Bi·∫øn d·∫°ng v√† k·∫øt h·ª£p nhi·ªÅu m·∫´u t·ª´ t·∫≠p ph·ª• tr·ª£ ƒë·ªÉ kh·ªõp v·ªõi observed points.
    - **Shen et al. [73]**: T√°i t·∫°o b·ªÅ m·∫∑t b·∫±ng c√°ch tr√≠ch xu·∫•t v√† l·∫Øp r√°p c√°c ph·∫ßn ri√™ng l·∫ª c·ªßa v·∫≠t th·ªÉ.

**V√≠ d·ª• trong nghi√™n c·ª©u**:

- **Semantic Segmentation**: Trong t√°i t·∫°o c·∫£nh (scene reconstruction), ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p n√†y c√≥ th·ªÉ g√°n t·ª´ng ph·∫ßn c·ªßa $P$ v√†o c√°c m·∫´u t∆∞∆°ng ·ª©ng v·ªõi c√°c v·∫≠t th·ªÉ c·ª• th·ªÉ, ch·∫≥ng h·∫°n nh∆∞ b√†n, gh·∫ø, ho·∫∑c c·ª≠a.
- **L·∫Øp r√°p m·∫´u (Part Assembly)**: Ph√π h·ª£p v·ªõi c√°c v·∫≠t th·ªÉ ph·ª©c t·∫°p kh√¥ng th·ªÉ bi·ªÉu di·ªÖn b·∫±ng m·ªôt m·∫´u duy nh·∫•t. C√°c ph·∫ßn nh·ªè ƒë∆∞·ª£c g·∫Øn k·∫øt l·∫°i ƒë·ªÉ t√°i t·∫°o to√†n b·ªô b·ªÅ m·∫∑t.

**∆Øu ƒëi·ªÉm**:

- Th√≠ch h·ª£p cho c√°c v·∫≠t th·ªÉ ho·∫∑c c·∫£nh ph·ª©c t·∫°p c√≥ c·∫•u tr√∫c ng·ªØ nghƒ©a.
- Cho ph√©p t√°i t·∫°o c√°c b·ªÅ m·∫∑t kh√¥ng th∆∞·ªùng xuy√™n ho·∫∑c kh√¥ng c√≥ m·∫´u h√¨nh h·ªçc r√µ r√†ng.

## Modeling Priors

**Modeling priors** l√† c√°c r√†ng bu·ªôc h√¨nh h·ªçc `geometry constraints` ƒë∆∞·ª£c cung c·∫•p b·ªüi ch√≠nh thi·∫øt k·∫ø c·ªßa c√°c m√¥ h√¨nh. Thay v√¨ ch·ªâ th√™m c√°c r√†ng bu·ªôc `regulizer` v√†o h√†m loss ho·∫∑c hypothesis space, c√°c thu·ªôc t√≠nh c·ªßa m√¥ h√¨nh (v√≠ d·ª•: m·∫°ng neural) ƒë∆∞·ª£c t·∫≠n d·ª•ng ƒë·ªÉ t·ª± ƒë·ªông √°p ƒë·∫∑t c√°c constraints. ƒêi·ªÅu n√†y gi√∫p t√°i t·∫°o b·ªÅ m·∫∑t $S$ ph√π h·ª£p v·ªõi h√¨nh h·ªçc c·ªßa d·ªØ li·ªáu.

M·ªôt v√≠ d·ª• ti√™u bi·ªÉu l√† **Deep Geometric Prior (DGP)**, ƒë∆∞·ª£c ph√°t tri·ªÉn t·ª´ √Ω t∆∞·ªüng **deep image prior**. C∆° ch·∫ø n√†y cho th·∫•y c√°c m·∫°ng deep neural c√≥ kh·∫£ nƒÉng t·ª± ƒë·ªông √°p ƒë·∫∑t c√°c r√†ng bu·ªôc h√¨nh h·ªçc ngay c·∫£ khi kh√¥ng ƒë∆∞·ª£c hu·∫•n luy·ªán. **Deep Geometric Prior**

[Deep Image Prior](https://dmitryulyanov.github.io/deep_image_prior)

- X√°c minh r·∫±ng c√°c m·∫°ng neural c√≥ th·ªÉ ƒë√≥ng vai tr√≤ nh∆∞ m·ªôt prior hi·ªáu qu·∫£ cho m√¥ h√¨nh h√≥a h√¨nh h·ªçc m√† kh√¥ng c·∫ßn qua qu√° tr√¨nh hu·∫•n luy·ªán.
- Thay v√¨ h·ªçc t·ª´ d·ªØ li·ªáu, m·∫°ng ƒë∆∞·ª£c s·ª≠ d·ª•ng nh∆∞ m·ªôt c√¥ng c·ª• ƒë·ªÉ kh·ªõp d·ªØ li·ªáu quan s√°t v·ªõi c√°c c·∫•u tr√∫c h√¨nh h·ªçc t·ª± nhi√™n.

<aside>
üí°

Motivated from deep image prior [74], Deep Geometric Prior (DGP) [75] verifies the efficacy of deep networks as a prior for geometric surface modeling, even when the networks are not trained.

</aside>

**C√°c ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p ph√°t tri·ªÉn t·ª´ DGP:**

**a. Point2Mesh [76] v√† SAIL-S3 [77]**: C·∫£ hai ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p m·ªü r·ªông DGP t·ª´ c·∫•p ƒë·ªô to√†n c·ª•c (global modeling) sang c·∫•p ƒë·ªô c·ª•c b·ªô (local modeling):

- **Point2Mesh**: X√¢y d·ª±ng c√°c h√†m ng·∫ßm c·ª•c b·ªô `global modeling adopted in [75] as local ones` d·ª±a tr√™n **MeshCNN**, trong ƒë√≥ c√°c tr·ªçng s·ªë ƒë∆∞·ª£c chia s·∫ª gi·ªØa c√°c ph·∫ßn c·ªßa m·∫°ng.
- **SAIL-S3**: S·ª≠ d·ª•ng **Multi-Layer Perceptron (MLP)** v·ªõi tr·ªçng s·ªë ƒë∆∞·ª£c chia s·∫ª ƒë·ªÉ x√¢y d·ª±ng c√°c h√†m ng·∫ßm c·ª•c b·ªô.

b. Deep Manifold Prior

- Ph√¢n t√≠ch to√°n h·ªçc c√°c ƒë·∫∑c t√≠nh c·ªßa MLP v√† m·∫°ng convolutional trong vi·ªác m√¥ h√¨nh h√≥a b·ªÅ m·∫∑t.
- Ch·ªâ ra r·∫±ng b·∫£n ch·∫•t c·ªßa c·∫•u tr√∫c m·∫°ng neural, ch·∫≥ng h·∫°n nh∆∞ c√°c layer ReLU, c√≥ th·ªÉ ho·∫°t ƒë·ªông nh∆∞ m·ªôt b·ªô regularizer.

Ngo√†i ra, **MLP v√† vai tr√≤ c·ªßa ReLU trong Modeling Priors. Atzmon et al. [80] c**h·ª©ng minh l√Ω thuy·∫øt r·∫±ng MLP v·ªõi **Rectified Linear Units (ReLUs)** c√≥ th·ªÉ t·∫°o ra c√°c b·ªÅ m·∫∑t **piecewise linear**. **Analytic Marching Algorithm** [81] ƒê·ªÅ xu·∫•t thu·∫≠t to√°n ƒë·ªÉ t√≠nh to√°n m·ªôt c√°ch gi·∫£i t√≠ch c√°c l∆∞·ªõi tam gi√°c (triangular mesh) t·ª´ c·∫•u tr√∫c c·ªßa MLP, cho th·∫•y c√°ch thi·∫øt k·∫ø m·∫°ng neural c√≥ th·ªÉ h√†nh x·ª≠ nh∆∞ m·ªôt m√¥ h√¨nh t√°i t·∫°o b·ªÅ m·∫∑t.

**C√°c ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p s·ª≠ d·ª•ng Modeling Priors kh√°c**

**a.  Implicit Geometric Regularization (IGR) [37]**: √Åp d·ª•ng r√†ng bu·ªôc b·ªï sung l√™n gradient c·ªßa m·∫°ng neural, gi√∫p b·ªÅ m·∫∑t ƒë∆∞·ª£c t√°i t·∫°o tr·ªü n√™n m∆∞·ª£t m√† h∆°n.

**b. Sign Agnostic Learning (SAL) [82] v√† bi·∫øn th·ªÉ [83], [84]**:

- T√°i t·∫°o b·ªÅ m·∫∑t t·ª´ point clouds kh√¥ng c√≥ ƒë·ªãnh h∆∞·ªõng (un-oriented point clouds) th√¥ng qua vi·ªác kh·ªüi t·∫°o ƒë·∫∑c bi·ªát c·ªßa m·∫°ng neural.
- **SSP [85]**: S·ª≠ d·ª•ng "semi-signed supervision" (gi√°m s√°t b√°n k√Ω hi·ªáu), ƒë∆∞·ª£c t·∫°o ra b·∫±ng c√°ch voxel h√≥a c√°c ƒëi·ªÉm kh√¥ng ƒë·ªãnh h∆∞·ªõng, nh·∫±m tr√°nh c√°c c·ª±c ti·ªÉu c·ª•c b·ªô kh√¥ng t·ªët.

**c. Neural Splines [87]**:

- T√°i t·∫°o b·ªÅ m·∫∑t d·ª±a tr√™n **random feature kernels** (h·∫°t nh√¢n ƒë·∫∑c tr∆∞ng ng·∫´u nhi√™n) t·ª´ c√°c m·∫°ng ReLU n√¥ng v·ªõi chi·ªÅu r·ªông v√¥ h·∫°n.
- Ch·ª©ng minh r·∫±ng c√°ch ti·∫øp c·∫≠n n√†y thi√™n v·ªÅ vi·ªác t√°i t·∫°o c√°c b·ªÅ m·∫∑t smooth

## **Learning-Based Priors**

**Learning-Based Priors**: L√† ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p h·ªçc c√°c **prior h√¨nh h·ªçc** t·ª´ m·ªôt t·∫≠p d·ªØ li·ªáu hu·∫•n luy·ªán g·ªìm c√°c c·∫∑p `learned from an auxiliary set of training shapes as optimized model parameters`, trong ƒë√≥:

$$
\{P_i, S_i^*\}_{i=1}^N
$$

- $P_i$: Observed Point Sets t·ª©c l√† c√°c t·∫≠p h·ª£p ƒëi·ªÉm $P_i = \{p_1, p_2, \dots, p_n\}$ thu th·∫≠p t·ª´ c√°c c·∫£m bi·∫øn 3D.
- $S_i^*$: ground-truth surfaces t∆∞∆°ng ·ª©ng v·ªõi point cloud $P_i$ l√† b·ªÅ m·∫∑t m√† ch√∫ng ta mu·ªën t√°i t·∫°o.

**√ù t∆∞·ªüng ch√≠nh**: H·ªçc c√°c tham s·ªë m√¥ h√¨nh ( $\theta_f$ ho·∫∑c $\theta_F$) t·ª´ t·∫≠p d·ªØ li·ªáu ƒë·ªÉ t√°i t·∫°o b·ªÅ m·∫∑t $S$ sao cho c√°c ƒë·∫∑c t√≠nh h√¨nh h·ªçc ƒë∆∞·ª£c ph√π h·ª£p.

**1. Bi·ªÉu di·ªÖn t∆∞·ªùng minh (Explicit Representation)**

Trong tr∆∞·ªùng h·ª£p bi·ªÉu di·ªÖn t∆∞·ªùng minh, ch√∫ng ta s·ª≠ d·ª•ng h√†m √°nh x·∫° $f(z, \tilde{\theta}_f)$, v·ªõi $\tilde{\theta}_f$ l√† c√°c tham s·ªë ƒë√£ h·ªçc t·ª´ t·∫≠p hu·∫•n luy·ªán.

$$
\min_z \mathcal{L}_{\text{exp}}\big(f(z; \tilde{\theta}_f); P\big) + \lambda \mathcal{R}_{\text{exp}}(z)
$$

Trong ƒë√≥:

- $f(z; \tilde{\theta}_f)$: H√†m √°nh x·∫° t∆∞·ªùng minh v·ªõi c√°c tham s·ªë ƒë√£ h·ªçc $\tilde{\theta}_f$, gi√∫p bi·∫øn ƒë·ªïi latent code $z$ th√†nh m·ªôt surface $S$
- $z$: Latent code, bi·ªÉu di·ªÖn h√¨nh d·∫°ng c·ªßa b·ªÅ m·∫∑t.
- $z$: R√†ng bu·ªôc ƒë·ªÉ tr√°nh overfitting, th∆∞·ªùng l√† chu·∫©n h√≥a $\|z\|$.

**Qu√° tr√¨nh h·ªçc tham s·ªë $\tilde{\theta}_f$:**

$$
\tilde{\theta}_f = \arg\min_{\theta_f} \frac{1}{N} \sum_{i=1}^N \mathcal{\tilde{L}}_{\text{exp}}(\theta_f; \{P_i, S_i^*\}) + \tilde{\lambda} \mathcal{\tilde{R}}_{\text{exp}}(\theta_f)
$$

- **√ù nghƒ©a**:
    - B∆∞·ªõc n√†y h·ªçc tham s·ªë m√¥ h√¨nh $\theta_f$ b·∫±ng c√°ch s·ª≠ d·ª•ng to√†n b·ªô t·∫≠p d·ªØ li·ªáu hu·∫•n luy·ªán sao cho b·ªÅ m·∫∑t t√°i t·∫°o g·∫ßn nh·∫•t v·ªõi b·ªÅ m·∫∑t th·ª±c t·∫ø $S_i^*$ v√† tr√°nh hi·ªán t∆∞∆°ng overfiiting
    - $\mathcal{\tilde{L}}_{\text{exp}}$: H√†m m·∫•t m√°t tr√™n t·∫≠p hu·∫•n luy·ªán (c√≥ th·ªÉ kh√°c v·ªõi $\mathcal{L}_{\text{exp}}$).
    - $\tilde{\lambda}$: ƒêi·ªÅu ch·ªânh m·ª©c ƒë·ªô ∆∞u ti√™n gi·ªØa overfitting v√† r√†ng bu·ªôc h√¨nh h·ªçc.

**2. Bi·ªÉu di·ªÖn ng·∫ßm (Implicit Representation)**

C√¥ng th·ª©c t·ªëi ∆∞u h√≥a v·ªõi implicit representation:

$$
\min_z \mathcal{L}_{\text{imp}}\big(F(z; \tilde{\theta}_F); P\big) + \lambda \mathcal{R}_{\text{imp}}(z)
$$

- $F(z; \tilde{\theta}_F)$: H√†m implicit, ƒë·ªãnh nghƒ©a b·ªÅ m·∫∑t qua zero-set level $F(q) = 0$ v·ªõi c√°c tham s·ªë ƒë√£ h·ªçc $\tilde{\theta}_F$

C√°c b∆∞·ªõc h·ªçc $\tilde{\theta}_F$ t∆∞∆°ng t·ª± nh∆∞ bi·ªÉu di·ªÖn t∆∞·ªùng minh:

$$
\tilde{\theta}_F = \arg\min_{\theta_F} \frac{1}{N} \sum_{i=1}^N \mathcal{\tilde{L}}_{\text{imp}}(\theta_F; \{P_i, S_i^*\}) + \tilde{\lambda} \mathcal{\tilde{R}}_{\text{imp}}(\theta_F)
$$

1. **Auto-Encoder trong h·ªçc tham s·ªë**

M·ªôt c·∫•u tr√∫c auto-encoder c√≥ th·ªÉ ƒë∆∞·ª£c s·ª≠ d·ª•ng ƒë·ªÉ h·ªçc tham s·ªë m√¥ h√¨nh. C·∫•u tr√∫c n√†y bao g·ªìm hai ph·∫ßn ch√≠nh encoder v√† decoder:

- $f_{\text{encoder}} \circ f_{\text{decoder}}$: K·∫øt h·ª£p encoder v√† decoder.
- Sau khi h·ªçc ƒë∆∞·ª£c $\tilde{\theta}_f = \{\tilde{\theta}_{f_{\text{encoder}}}, \tilde{\theta}_{f_{\text{decoder}}}\}$, latent code $z$ c√≥ th·ªÉ ƒë∆∞·ª£c l·∫•y tr·ª±c ti·∫øp t·ª´:

$$
z = f_{\text{encoder}}(P; \tilde{\theta}_{f_{\text{encoder}}})
$$

Quy tr√¨nh n√†y c≈©ng √°p d·ª•ng t∆∞∆°ng t·ª± cho h√†m implicit $F$
:

$$
z = F_{\text{encoder}}(P; \tilde{\theta}_{F_{\text{encoder}}})
$$

**∆Øu ƒëi·ªÉm c·ªßa auto-encoder**:

- T√°ch bi·ªát gi·ªØa vi·ªác h·ªçc tham s·ªë v√† t·ªëi ∆∞u h√≥a latent code, gi√∫p qu√° tr√¨nh h·ªçc tr·ªü n√™n hi·ªáu qu·∫£ h∆°n.
- Gi·∫£m thi·ªÉu chi ph√≠ t√≠nh to√°n v√† t·ªëi ∆∞u h√≥a.

**Hai c·∫•p ƒë·ªô h·ªçc Prior bao g·ªìm:**

### **1. Semantic Priors**

**Semantic Priors** l√† vi·ªác h·ªçc c√°c ƒë·∫∑c tr∆∞ng ng·ªØ nghƒ©a (semantic features) chung cho m·ªôt danh m·ª•c ƒë·ªëi t∆∞·ª£ng (category). C·ª• th·ªÉ, n√≥ h·ªçc c√°c m√¥ h√¨nh h√¨nh h·ªçc cho c√°c lo·∫°i ƒë·ªëi t∆∞·ª£ng c·ª• th·ªÉ.

- **V√≠ d·ª•**:
    - **Deep Marching Cubes** [88]: K·∫øt n·ªëi m·∫°ng neural v·ªõi thu·∫≠t to√°n Marching Cubes qua m·ªôt l·ªõp ph√¢n t√≠ch kh·∫£ vi, gi√∫p t√°i t·∫°o b·ªÅ m·∫∑t v·ªõi prior ng·ªØ nghƒ©a.
    - **OccNet** [9] v√† **IM-Net** [91]: S·ª≠ d·ª•ng auto-encoder ƒë·ªÉ h·ªçc global latent code, sau ƒë√≥ d·ª± ƒëo√°n kh·∫£ nƒÉng t·ªìn t·∫°i ƒëi·ªÉm tr√™n b·ªÅ m·∫∑t (**occupancy)** ho·∫∑c **signed distance**.
- **∆Øu ƒëi·ªÉm**:
    - D·ªÖ d√†ng kh√°i qu√°t h√≥a c√°c h√¨nh d·∫°ng thu·ªôc c√πng m·ªôt lo·∫°i ƒë·ªëi t∆∞·ª£ng.
    - √Åp d·ª•ng ƒë∆∞·ª£c cho c√°c b√†i to√°n v·ªõi √≠t th√¥ng tin 3D, v√≠ d·ª•: t√°i t·∫°o t·ª´ h√¨nh ·∫£nh RGB [5].

### **2. Local Shape Primitives**

Khi ƒë·ªëi t∆∞·ª£ng kh√¥ng th·ªÉ ƒë∆∞·ª£c ph√¢n lo·∫°i v√†o danh m·ª•c c·ªë ƒë·ªãnh, ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p n√†y h·ªçc c√°c **h√¨nh d·∫°ng c·ª•c b·ªô** (local shape primitives), c√≥ th·ªÉ ƒë∆∞·ª£c √°p d·ª•ng cho c√°c ƒë·ªëi t∆∞·ª£ng ph·ª©c t·∫°p ho·∫∑c kh√¥ng r√µ r√†ng v·ªÅ ng·ªØ nghƒ©a.

- C√°c ƒë·ªëi t∆∞·ª£ng kh√¥ng thu·ªôc danh m·ª•c c·ªë ƒë·ªãnh.
- B·ªÅ m·∫∑t ph·ª©c t·∫°p v·ªõi nhi·ªÅu chi ti·∫øt nh·ªè.

**V√≠ d·ª• v·ªÅ ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p**:

- **IF-Net** [101]: S·ª≠ d·ª•ng 3D convolution ƒë·ªÉ h·ªçc latent code cho t·ª´ng local grid.
- **DeepLS** [34]: Hu·∫•n luy·ªán h√†m implicit chia s·∫ª tham s·ªë gi·ªØa c√°c local voxel.
- **PatchNets** [33]: H·ªçc c√°c ƒë·∫∑c tr∆∞ng c·ªßa t·ª´ng patch b·ªÅ m·∫∑t b·∫±ng c·∫•u tr√∫c implicit auto-decoder.

**∆Øu ƒëi·ªÉm**:

- Linh ho·∫°t h∆°n trong vi·ªác t√°i t·∫°o c√°c h√¨nh d·∫°ng kh√¥ng ƒë·ªìng nh·∫•t.
- TƒÉng kh·∫£ nƒÉng m√¥ h√¨nh h√≥a chi ti·∫øt nh·ªè.

## **Hybrid Priors**

Trong ph·∫ßn n√†y, t√°c gi·∫£ th·∫£o lu·∫≠n v·ªÅ c√°c ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p s·ª≠ d·ª•ng **r√†ng bu·ªôc h√¨nh h·ªçc k·∫øt h·ª£p** (*hybrid priors*), k·∫øt h·ª£p nhi·ªÅu chi·∫øn l∆∞·ª£c kh√°c nhau ƒë·ªÉ c·∫£i thi·ªán ƒë·ªô tin c·∫≠y v√† t√≠nh h·ª£p l√Ω c·ªßa b·ªÅ m·∫∑t t√°i t·∫°o (reconstructed surface). C·ª• th·ªÉ, m·ª•c ti√™u l√† s·ª≠ d·ª•ng c√°c learning-based **priors** k·∫øt h·ª£p v·ªõi c√°c **existing method** ƒë·ªÉ ƒë·∫°t ƒë∆∞·ª£c k·∫øt qu·∫£ t√°i t·∫°o ch√≠nh x√°c h∆°n v√† h·ª£p l√Ω h∆°n, ƒë·∫∑c bi·ªát l√† trong **deep learning era**. D∆∞·ªõi ƒë√¢y l√† ph·∫ßn ph√¢n t√≠ch chi ti·∫øt v√† gi·∫£i th√≠ch c√°c v√≠ d·ª• m√† t√°c gi·∫£ ƒë∆∞a ra trong ph·∫ßn n√†y.

**1. C√°c chi·∫øn l∆∞·ª£c k·∫øt h·ª£p priors**

C√°c ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p trong lƒ©nh v·ª±c t√°i t·∫°o b·ªÅ m·∫∑t c√≥ th·ªÉ ƒë∆∞·ª£c ph√¢n lo·∫°i theo c√°c lo·∫°i **priors h√¨nh h·ªçc** m√† ch√∫ng s·ª≠ d·ª•ng. ƒê·ªÉ c·∫£i thi·ªán t√≠nh h·ª£p l√Ω c·ªßa c√°c b·ªÅ m·∫∑t t√°i t·∫°o, c√°c ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p hi·ªán t·∫°i th∆∞·ªùng **k·∫øt h·ª£p nhi·ªÅu priors**:

- **K·∫øt h·ª£p priors smoothness v·ªõi priors triangulation ho·∫∑c template-based**.
- **K·∫øt h·ª£p c√°c templated-based priors v·ªõi c√°c learning-based priors** ƒë·ªÉ c·∫£i thi·ªán ch·∫•t l∆∞·ª£ng reconstruction.
- C√°c ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p k·∫øt h·ª£p n√†y tr·ªü n√™n ph·ªï bi·∫øn khi s·ª≠ d·ª•ng **deep learning** cho t√°i t·∫°o b·ªÅ m·∫∑t t·ª´ c√°c point cloud.

**2. K·∫øt h·ª£p priors h·ªçc ƒë∆∞·ª£c v·ªõi priors triangulation (D·ª±a tr√™n l∆∞·ªõi tam gi√°c)**

C√°c ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p k·∫øt h·ª£p priors h·ªçc ƒë∆∞·ª£c v√† **Delaunay triangulation** l√† m·ªôt v√≠ d·ª• r√µ r√†ng. C√°c deep-learning network ƒë∆∞·ª£c hu·∫•n luy·ªán ƒë·ªÉ r√∫t ra c√°c ƒë·∫∑c ƒëi·ªÉm h√¨nh h·ªçc t·ª´ point cloud v√† s·ª≠ d·ª•ng ch√∫ng ƒë·ªÉ t·∫°o ra c√°c triangular mesh cho b·ªÅ m·∫∑t t√°i t·∫°o.

**ƒêi·ªÉn h√¨nh: PointTriNet (Point Triangulation Network)**

- **PointTriNet** l√† m·ªôt framework s·ª≠ d·ª•ng **proposal network** ƒë·ªÉ ƒë∆∞a ra c√°c candidates of triangle v√† **classification network** ƒë·ªÉ x√°c ƒë·ªãnh xem c√°c candidates n√†y c√≥ ph·∫£i l√† m·ªôt ph·∫ßn c·ªßa surface reconstruction hay kh√¥ng.
- C√°c b∆∞·ªõc ho·∫°t ƒë·ªông c·ªßa PointTriNet:
    - **Proposal network**: ƒê·ªÅ xu·∫•t c√°c triangles t·ª´ c√°c ƒëi·ªÉm trong Point Cloud Set.
    - **Classification network**: D·ª± ƒëo√°n xem li·ªáu m·ªôt tam gi√°c c√≥ n·∫±m trong b·ªÅ m·∫∑t t√°i t·∫°o hay kh√¥ng.
    - **Iterative effect**: Hai m·∫°ng n√†y l√†m vi·ªác tu·∫ßn t·ª± cho ƒë·∫øn khi b·ªÅ m·∫∑t cu·ªëi c√πng ƒë∆∞·ª£c t·∫°o ra d∆∞·ªõi d·∫°ng l∆∞·ªõi tam gi√°c.

**‚Üí √ù nghƒ©a**: Ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p n√†y gi√∫p t√°i t·∫°o b·ªÅ m·∫∑t t·ª´ ƒë√°m m√¢y ƒëi·ªÉm th√¥ng qua vi·ªác x√¢y d·ª±ng c√°c tam gi√°c, s·ª≠ d·ª•ng m·∫°ng h·ªçc s√¢u ƒë·ªÉ t·ªëi ∆∞u h√≥a v√† ch·ªçn l·ª±a c√°c tam gi√°c ph√π h·ª£p.

**3. Delaunay Surface Elements (DSE)**

M·ªôt ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p kh√°c l√† **Delaunay Surface Elements (DSE)**, k·∫øt h·ª£p **Delaunay triangulation** v·ªõi c√°c **logarithmic maps** h·ªçc ƒë∆∞·ª£c ƒë·ªÉ t·∫°o ra c√°c m·∫£nh tam gi√°c nh·ªè.

- C√°c **logarithmic maps** h·ªçc ƒë∆∞·ª£c gi√∫p ƒëi·ªÅu ch·ªânh c√°c ƒë·∫∑c ƒëi·ªÉm h√¨nh h·ªçc c·ªßa b·ªÅ m·∫∑t, ƒë·∫£m b·∫£o b·ªÅ m·∫∑t t√°i t·∫°o h·ª£p l√Ω h∆°n.
- **Adaptive voting algorithm**: M·ªôt thu·∫≠t to√°n b·∫ßu ch·ªçn th√≠ch nghi ƒë·ªÉ ch·ªçn c√°c tam gi√°c ·ª©ng vi√™n ph√π h·ª£p t·ª´ c√°c m·∫£nh tam gi√°c ƒë∆∞·ª£c t·∫°o ra.

**4. DeepDT (Deep Delaunay Tetrahedrons)**

Ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p **DeepDT** s·ª≠ d·ª•ng **deep learning** ƒë·ªÉ h·ªçc c√°c ƒë·∫∑c ƒëi·ªÉm h√¨nh h·ªçc t·ª´ point cloud, sau ƒë√≥ k·∫øt h·ª£p v·ªõi th√¥ng graph structural information ƒë·ªÉ x√°c ƒë·ªãnh c√°c **labels b√™n trong/ngo√†i** c·ªßa **Delaunay tetrahedrons**. Sau ƒë√≥, b·ªÅ m·∫∑t ƒë∆∞·ª£c t√°i t·∫°o b·∫±ng c√°ch **l·∫•y c√°c m·∫∑t tam gi√°c** gi·ªØa c√°c tetrahedrons c√≥ **labels kh√°c nhau** (inside/outside).

**‚Üí √ù nghƒ©a**: Ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p n√†y s·ª≠ d·ª•ng c√°c **Delaunay tetrahedrons** v√† c√°c k·ªπ thu·∫≠t h·ªçc s√¢u ƒë·ªÉ c·∫£i thi·ªán vi·ªác x√°c ƒë·ªãnh c√°c m·∫∑t tam gi√°c v√† b·ªÅ m·∫∑t t√°i t·∫°o.

**5. T√°i t·∫°o b·ªÅ m·∫∑t v·ªõi D·ª± ƒëo√°n c√°c v·ªã tr√≠ ƒë·ªânh c·ªßa tetrahedrons**

**Gao et al. (2019)** [127] s·ª≠ d·ª•ng deep-learning network ƒë·ªÉ d·ª± ƒëo√°n **offsets** (s·ª± d·ªãch chuy·ªÉn) c·ªßa c√°c ƒë·ªânh c·ªßa **tetrahedrons**, c√πng v·ªõi m·ªôt m·∫°ng kh√°c ƒë·ªÉ d·ª± ƒëo√°n **occupancy** (t√≠nh ƒë·∫ßy ƒë·ªß) c·ªßa t·ª´ng tetrahedron. B·ªÅ m·∫∑t c·ªßa v·∫≠t th·ªÉ ƒë∆∞·ª£c t·∫°o ra t·ª´ **m·∫∑t c·ªßa hai tetrahedrons** c√≥ **occupancy kh√°c nhau**.

**‚Üí √ù nghƒ©a**: Ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p n√†y gi√∫p d·ª± ƒëo√°n v·ªã tr√≠ c·ªßa c√°c ƒë·ªânh v√† t√≠nh ch·∫•t c·ªßa c√°c **tetrahedrons** ƒë·ªÉ x√¢y d·ª±ng b·ªÅ m·∫∑t.

**6. K·∫øt h·ª£p priors h·ªçc ƒë∆∞·ª£c v·ªõi priors ƒë·ªô tr∆°n (Smoothness Priors)**

M·ªôt c√°ch k·∫øt h·ª£p ph·ªï bi·∫øn l√† k·∫øt h·ª£p **priors h·ªçc ƒë∆∞·ª£c** v·ªõi **priors ƒë·ªô tr∆°n**:

- **Laplacian regularization**: ƒê∆∞·ª£c s·ª≠ d·ª•ng ƒë·ªÉ ƒë·∫£m b·∫£o b·ªÅ m·∫∑t t√°i t·∫°o c√≥ smooth, gi·∫£m thi·ªÉu c√°c g·ªì gh·ªÅ ho·∫∑c nh·∫•p nh√¥.
- **Cosine smoothness**: M·ªôt d·∫°ng regularization kh√°c gi√∫p l√†m m·ªãn b·ªÅ m·∫∑t.

**ƒêi·ªÉn h√¨nh: IMLSNet**

- **IMLSNet** l√† m·ªôt m·∫°ng h·ªçc s√¢u s·ª≠ d·ª•ng **implicit network** ƒë·ªÉ t√≠nh to√°n kho·∫£ng c√°ch c√≥ d·∫•u (signed distances) t·∫°i c√°c l∆∞·ªõi trong kh√¥ng gian 3D theo m√¥ h√¨nh **octree**.
- ƒê·ªô tr∆°n c·ªßa b·ªÅ m·∫∑t ƒë∆∞·ª£c ƒëi·ªÅu ch·ªânh b·∫±ng c√°ch ƒë·ªãnh nghƒ©a c√°c **signed distances** t∆∞∆°ng t·ª± nh∆∞ trong **implicit moving least squares (MLS)**.

**7. K·∫øt h·ª£p priors h·ªçc ƒë∆∞·ª£c v·ªõi priors d·ª±a tr√™n template**

C√°c ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p k·∫øt h·ª£p **priors h·ªçc ƒë∆∞·ª£c** v·ªõi **template-based priors**:

- **SPFN (Surface Prediction from Network)**: ƒê√†o t·∫°o m·ªôt deep-learning network ƒë·ªÉ ph√π h·ª£p v·ªõi c√°c **primitive geometry** (h√¨nh h·ªçc nguy√™n th·ªßy), v√≠ d·ª• nh∆∞ c√°c kh·ªëi h√¨nh h·ªçc c∆° b·∫£n (h√¨nh c·∫ßu, h√¨nh h·ªôp, v.v.).
- **CPFN (Combined Primitive Fitting Network)**: H·ªçc hai m·∫°ng SPFNs: m·ªôt m·∫°ng cho c√°c **primitive l·ªõn** v√† m·ªôt m·∫°ng cho c√°c **primitive nh·ªè**.
- **ParseNet**: S·ª≠ d·ª•ng m·ªôt **neural decomposition module** ƒë·ªÉ ph√¢n t√°ch ƒë√°m m√¢y ƒëi·ªÉm th√†nh nhi·ªÅu ph·∫ßn con, m·ªói ph·∫ßn ƒë∆∞·ª£c gi·∫£ ƒë·ªãnh l√† m·ªôt **primitive** v√† ƒë∆∞·ª£c m√¥ h√¨nh h√≥a b·∫±ng **B-splines**.

**8. Local Deep Implicit Function (LDIF)**

**LDIF** ƒë·∫°i di·ªán cho b·ªÅ m·∫∑t d∆∞·ªõi d·∫°ng **a set of shape elements**, m·ªói ph·∫ßn t·ª≠ ƒë∆∞·ª£c parameterized b·∫±ng c√°c analytic shape variables v√† latent shape codes. **SIF encoder** v√† **PointNet encoder** ƒë∆∞·ª£c s·ª≠ d·ª•ng ƒë·ªÉ h·ªçc c√°c bi·∫øn h√¨nh h·ªçc v√† m√£ h√≥a ·∫©n.

**‚Üí √ù nghƒ©a**: Ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p n√†y cho ph√©p t√°i t·∫°o c√°c b·ªÅ m·∫∑t ph·ª©c t·∫°p v√† c√°c h√¨nh h·ªçc kh√¥ng gian l·ªõn b·∫±ng c√°ch s·ª≠ d·ª•ng c√°c m·∫°ng h·ªçc s√¢u ƒë·ªÉ h·ªçc c√°c ƒë·∫∑c tr∆∞ng h√¨nh h·ªçc.

**9. RetrievalFuse**

**RetrievalFuse** s·ª≠ d·ª•ng m·ªôt b·ªô d·ªØ li·ªáu template c√°c v·∫≠t th·ªÉ ƒë·ªÉ **truy xu·∫•t** c√°c m·∫´u t·ª´ m·ªôt b·ªô auxiliary scene dataset v√† s·ª≠ d·ª•ng m·ªôt m·∫°ng deep-learning c√≥ **attention-based refinement** ƒë·ªÉ tinh ch·ªânh b·ªÅ m·∫∑t t√°i t·∫°o t·ª´ c√°c template.

**‚Üí √ù nghƒ©a**: Ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p n√†y s·ª≠ d·ª•ng vi·ªác **truy xu·∫•t th√¥ng tin t·ª´ b·ªô d·ªØ li·ªáu h·ªó tr·ª£** `auxiliary dataset` ƒë·ªÉ gi√∫p t√°i t·∫°o b·ªÅ m·∫∑t cho c√°c scences quy m√¥ l·ªõn.

**Details**

- [**Mesh 3d ? Type of Mesh ?**](https://www.notion.so/Mesh-3d-Type-of-Mesh-1462a3f8f2a180c39b65ef99f21c26a2?pvs=21)

# Benchmark

T√°c gi·∫£ b√†i b√°o ƒë√£ ƒë·ªÅ xu·∫•t m·ªôt **benchmarking pipeline** chi ti·∫øt ƒë·ªÉ t·∫°o ra d·ªØ li·ªáu t·ªïng h·ª£p (synthetic data) cho c√°c b√†i to√°n t√°i t·∫°o b·ªÅ m·∫∑t (surface reconstruction) t·ª´ Point Cloud. Ph·∫ßn n√†y t·∫≠p trung v√†o d·ªØ li·ªáu c√°c v·∫≠t th·ªÉ (object surfaces) v√† c·∫£nh (scences) ƒë∆∞·ª£c t·ªïng h·ª£p v·ªõi nh·ªØng ƒë·∫∑c ƒëi·ªÉm sau:

1. ƒê∆∞·ª£c t·ªï ch·ª©c d·ª±a tr√™n level complex of surface.
2. Bao g·ªìm c·∫£ d·ªØ li·ªáu qu√©t l√Ω t∆∞·ªüng (perfect scanning) v√† d·ªØ li·ªáu ch·ª©a c√°c l·ªói th∆∞·ªùng g·∫∑p trong th·ª±c t·∫ø.

M·ª•c ti√™u c·ªßa benchmark l√†:

- T·∫°o ra b·ªô d·ªØ li·ªáu synthetic chu·∫©n h√≥a bao g·ªìm c√°c b·ªÅ m·∫∑t v·∫≠t th·ªÉ c√≥ ƒë·ªô ph·ª©c t·∫°p kh√°c nhau.
- M√¥ ph·ªèng c√°c l·ªói th∆∞·ªùng g·∫∑p trong qu√° tr√¨nh qu√©t th·ª±c t·∫ø, bao g·ªìm:
    - Nhi·ªÖu ƒëi·ªÉm (point-wise noise).
    - Ph√¢n b·ªë kh√¥ng ƒë·ªìng ƒë·ªÅu (non-uniform distribution).
    - ƒêi·ªÉm ngo·∫°i lai (point outliers).
    - Sai l·ªách v·ªã tr√≠ qu√©t (misalignment).
    - M·∫•t ƒëi·ªÉm d·ªØ li·ªáu (missing points).

‚Üí B·ªô d·ªØ li·ªáu n√†y cung c·∫•p m·ªôt m√¥i tr∆∞·ªùng ƒë·ªÉ so s√°nh c√°c thu·∫≠t to√°n surface reconstruction m·ªôt c√°ch to√†n di·ªán.

## **The Synthetic Data of Object Surfaces**

![Screenshot 2024-11-23 at 16.11.12.png](Surface%20Reconstruction%20From%20Point%20Clouds%20A%20Survey%20%201442a3f8f2a180aca990fd4b2793fb3b/Screenshot_2024-11-23_at_16.11.12.png)

Section n√†y tr√¨nh b√†y quy tr√¨nh x√¢y d·ª±ng **d·ªØ li·ªáu t·ªïng h·ª£p (synthetic data)** nh·∫±m h·ªó tr·ª£ ƒë√°nh gi√° c√°c ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p surface reconstruction. T√°c gi·∫£ m√¥ t·∫£ c√°ch t·∫°o ra d·ªØ li·ªáu t·ª´ c√°c [CAD Model](https://www.notion.so/CAD-Model-1472a3f8f2a1809292f5c57c1f4a21a3?pvs=21) b·∫±ng c√°ch gi·∫£ l·∫≠p nhi·ªÅu t√¨nh hu·ªëng scanning kh√°c nhau ƒë·ªÉ ph·∫£n √°nh c√°c ƒëi·ªÅu ki·ªán th·ª±c t·∫ø. B√™n c·∫°nh ƒë√≥, d·ªØ li·ªáu n√†y ƒë∆∞·ª£c ph√¢n lo·∫°i theo ƒë·ªô ph·ª©c t·∫°p b·ªÅ m·∫∑t `complex surface` ƒë·ªÉ ph√¢n t√≠ch hi·ªáu nƒÉng c·ªßa c√°c ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p trong c√°c tr∆∞·ªùng h·ª£p kh√°c nhau. D∆∞·ªõi ƒë√¢y l√† gi·∫£i th√≠ch v√† ph√¢n t√≠ch chi ti·∫øt t·ª´ng n·ªôi dung quan tr·ªçng.

T√°c gi·∫£ ƒë√£ x√¢y d·ª±ng m·ªôt **benchmark** to√†n di·ªán ƒë·ªÉ ƒë√°nh gi√° c√°c ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p surface reconstruction. B·ªô d·ªØ li·ªáu t·ªïng h·ª£p n√†y bao g·ªìm:

- C√°c CAD models v·ªõi ba m·ª©c ƒë·ªô ph·ª©c t·∫°p b·ªÅ m·∫∑t (`low`, `middle`, `high`).
- C√°c t√¨nh hu·ªëng qu√©t th·ª±c t·∫ø ƒë∆∞·ª£c m√¥ ph·ªèng chi ti·∫øt (5 d·∫°ng l·ªói qu√©t).

### **1. Thu th·∫≠p v√† ti·ªÅn x·ª≠ l√Ω d·ªØ li·ªáu CAD**

T√°c gi·∫£ s·ª≠ d·ª•ng c√°c **CAD models** t·ª´ c√°c data repository *[**Dataset**](https://www.notion.so/Dataset-1452a3f8f2a18007b376d1ccbb94ed15?pvs=21)* hi·ªán c√≥:

- **Thingi10k [22]**: M·ªôt b·ªô d·ªØ li·ªáu g·ªìm c√°c m√¥ h√¨nh in 3D ƒë∆∞·ª£c chia s·∫ª tr·ª±c tuy·∫øn, v·ªõi 3,000 objects ƒë∆∞·ª£c ch·ªçn ng·∫´u nhi√™n.
- **ABC [21]**: Ch·ªçn 3,000 th√†nh ph·∫ßn c√¥ng nghi·ªáp t·ª´ t·∫≠p **Chunk 0080**.
- **3DNet Cat200 [20]**: G·ªìm 3,400 h√†ng h√≥a th∆∞∆°ng m·∫°i.
- **Three D Scans [23]**: G·ªìm 106 t√°c ph·∫©m ƒëi√™u kh·∫Øc ngh·ªá thu·∫≠t.

‚Üí T·ªïng c·ªông c√≥ **9,506 CAD models** ƒë∆∞·ª£c thu th·∫≠p.

1. **Lo·∫°i b·ªè c√°c tr∆∞·ªùng h·ª£p kh√¥ng ph√π h·ª£p**:
    - M·ªôt s·ªë **meshes** kh√¥ng ƒë√°p ·ª©ng ƒëi·ªÅu ki·ªán **watertight** (k√≠n n∆∞·ªõc), **2D-manifold** (m·∫∑t 2D li√™n t·ª•c), ho·∫∑c qu√° ph·ª©c t·∫°p v·ªÅ m·∫∑t topology (**self-occlusion** v√† surface genus cao). ***[**Non-wateright, Self-occlusion, 2D -manifold,  Surface Genus**](https://www.notion.so/Non-wateright-Self-occlusion-2D-manifold-Surface-Genus-1472a3f8f2a18047bff1d503bbf5fa9d?pvs=21)***
    - C√°c ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p ki·ªÉm tra bao g·ªìm:
        - Ki·ªÉm tra tr·∫°ng th√°i **watertight** v√† **2D-manifold** [135].
        - Ki·ªÉm tra **self-occlusion** [136].
        - T√≠nh to√°n **surface genus** [32].
2. **Normalization**:
    - C√°c **meshes** c√≤n l·∫°i ƒë∆∞·ª£c ƒë∆∞a v·ªÅ tr·∫°ng th√°i chu·∫©n ho√°:
        - **ƒê·∫∑t t√¢m t·∫°i g·ªëc t·ªça ƒë·ªô**.
        - **Co gi√£n isotropically** ƒë·ªÉ n·∫±m trong m·ªôt h√¨nh c·∫ßu ƒë∆°n v·ªã. ***[**Istrophy**](https://www.notion.so/Istrophy-1472a3f8f2a1806d9de4f8d0d472316b?pvs=21)***

‚Üí **K·∫øt qu·∫£**: Sau khi l·ªçc v√† x·ª≠ l√Ω, **1,620 object surface meshes** ƒë∆∞·ª£c gi·ªØ l·∫°i ƒë·ªÉ ƒë∆∞a v√†o b·ªô d·ªØ li·ªáu **benchmark**.

### **2. Ph√¢n nh√≥m theo ƒë·ªô ph·ª©c t·∫°p b·ªÅ m·∫∑t**

T√°c gi·∫£ ph√¢n t√≠ch r·∫±ng performance c·ªßa c√°c ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p surface reconstruction c√≥ th·ªÉ ph·ª• thu·ªôc v√†o **ƒë·ªô ph·ª©c t·∫°p c·ªßa b·ªÅ m·∫∑t** `complexities of object surfaces`. Do ƒë√≥, c√°c ƒë·ªëi t∆∞·ª£ng ƒë∆∞·ª£c chia th√†nh ba nh√≥m d·ª±a tr√™n **algebraic complexity** (ƒë·ªô ph·ª©c t·∫°p ƒë·∫°i s·ªë).

**ƒêo l∆∞·ªùng ƒë·ªô ph·ª©c t·∫°p [Algebraic Complexity, Topological Complexity](https://www.notion.so/Algebraic-Complexity-Topological-Complexity-1472a3f8f2a180d890bce97882e233d4?pvs=21)** 

- **Algebraic complexity**: ƒêo ƒë·ªô ph·ª©c t·∫°p ƒë·∫°i s·ªë d·ª±a tr√™n **b·∫≠c cao nh·∫•t c·ªßa ƒëa th·ª©c (polynomial degree)** d√πng ƒë·ªÉ x·∫•p x·ªâ c√°c m·∫£nh b·ªÅ m·∫∑t c·ª•c b·ªô.
- **Topological complexity**: ƒê∆∞·ª£c ƒëo b·∫±ng **surface genus** (s·ªë l·ªó tr√™n b·ªÅ m·∫∑t).

> L∆∞u √Ω: C√°c meshes ƒë√£ ƒë∆∞·ª£c x·ª≠ l√Ω ƒë·ªÉ ƒë·∫£m b·∫£o:
> 
> - Watertight.
> - 2D-manifold.
> - Genus ‚â§ 5 (topology ƒë∆°n gi·∫£n).

**Ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p chia nh√≥m**

- **Kh√≥ khƒÉn c·ªßa vi·ªác ƒëo l∆∞·ªùng**: X·∫•p x·ªâ b·∫±ng ƒëa th·ª©c b·∫≠c cao th∆∞·ªùng kh√¥ng ·ªïn ƒë·ªãnh [60] v√† d·ªÖ g√¢y l·ªói d·ª± ƒëo√°n.
- **Gi·∫£i ph√°p**: T√°c gi·∫£ s·ª≠ d·ª•ng m·ªôt chi·∫øn l∆∞·ª£c kh√°c:
    - Gi·ªØ c·ªë ƒë·ªãnh b·∫≠c ƒëa th·ª©c cao nh·∫•t.
    - ƒêo l∆∞·ªùng **sai s·ªë x·∫•p x·ªâ trung b√¨nh** (average approximation errors) tr√™n c√°c m·∫£nh b·ªÅ m·∫∑t c·ª•c b·ªô.

<aside>
üí°

However, given fixed budget of approximation errors, it is usually unstable to fit local surface patches with polynomials of high degrees [60], causing inaccurate prediction of polynomial degrees and thus that of algebraic complexity. Instead, we take the strategy of fixing the highest function degree and measuring the averaged approximation errors of local surface patches; technical details are given in Appendix A, available online.

</aside>

**Ph√¢n nh√≥m**

- Ba nh√≥m ƒë∆∞·ª£c chia theo t·ª∑ l·ªá **6:3:1**:
    - **Low-complexity**: 972 instances.
    - **Middle-complexity**: 486 instances.
    - **High-complexity**: 162 instances.

### **3. Qu√©t d·ªØ li·ªáu t·ªïng h·ª£p t·ª´ CAD models**

T√°c gi·∫£ s·ª≠ d·ª•ng **Blender Sensor Simulation Toolbox (BlenSor) [137]** ƒë·ªÉ m√¥ ph·ªèng c√°c ƒëi·ªÅu ki·ªán qu√©t d·ªØ li·ªáu, bao g·ªìm c·∫£ `perfect scanning` v√† kh√¥ng ho√†n h·∫£o. Quy tr√¨nh c·ª• th·ªÉ ƒë∆∞·ª£c m√¥ t·∫£ nh∆∞ sau:

**Perfect Scanning**

1. **ƒê·∫∑t camera TOF (Time-of-Flight)**:
    - Camera ƒë∆∞·ª£c ƒë·∫∑t tr√™n c√°c **v√≤ng c·∫ßu (viewing spheres)** c√≥ b√°n k√≠nh t·ª´ $r_{min}=2.5$ **ƒë·∫øn $r_{max}=3.5$**.
    - M·ªôt ƒëi·ªÉm quan s√°t ƒë∆∞·ª£c x√°c ƒë·ªãnh b·ªüi **camera extrinsic matrix K = [R|t]**.
2. **Qu√©t t·ª´ nhi·ªÅu g√≥c nh√¨n**:
    - T√°c gi·∫£ s·ª≠ d·ª•ng **1,000 viewpoints** tr√™n c√°c v√≤ng c·∫ßu ƒë·ªÉ thu th·∫≠p c√°c point clouds bao ph·ªß t·ª´ng ph·∫ßn b·ªÅ m·∫∑t.
    - C√°c point clouds ri√™ng l·∫ª n√†y ƒë∆∞·ª£c `register` v√† `fuse` ƒë·ªÉ t·∫°o ra m·ªôt point cloud ƒë·∫ßy ƒë·ªß bao ph·ªß to√†n b·ªô b·ªÅ m·∫∑t.
3. **ƒêi·ªÅu ch·ªânh density**: √Åp d·ª•ng **Farthest Point Sampling (FPS)** ƒë·ªÉ ƒë·∫£m b·∫£o m·∫≠t ƒë·ªô ƒëi·ªÉm ƒë·ªìng ƒë·ªÅu **[Farthest Point Sampling (FPS)](https://www.notion.so/Farthest-Point-Sampling-FPS-1472a3f8f2a1802ebe2de1bd22cfcdf5?pvs=21)** 
    - **80k points**: Low-complexity.
    - **120k points**: Middle-complexity.
    - **160k points**: High-complexity.
4. **T√≠nh to√°n surface normals**: S·ª≠ d·ª•ng **PCA** tr√™n l√¢n c·∫≠n **k=40 nearest neighbors** ƒë·ªÉ t√≠nh to√°n c√°c **normals**.

**Imperfect Scanning (5 lo·∫°i l·ªói qu√©t):**

1. **Point-wise noise**: M√¥ ph·ªèng **nhi·ªÖu ƒëi·ªÉm ƒë·ªôc l·∫≠p** b·∫±ng c√°ch th√™m nhi·ªÖu Gaussian v·ªõi m·ª©c ƒë·ªô kh√°c nhau $œÉ_{noise} = [0.001, 0.003, 0.006]$.
2. **Non-uniform distribution**: S·ª≠ d·ª•ng **Random Sampling (RS)** thay v√¨ FPS ƒë·ªÉ t·∫°o m·∫≠t ƒë·ªô ƒëi·ªÉm kh√¥ng ƒë·ªìng ƒë·ªÅu.
3. **Point outliers**: Th√™m **outliers** b·∫±ng c√°ch d·ªãch chuy·ªÉn m·ªôt s·ªë ƒëi·ªÉm (t·ª∑ l·ªá $outlier = [0.1\%, 0.3\%, 0.6\%]$) kh·ªèi b·ªÅ m·∫∑t v·ªõi kho·∫£ng c√°ch x√°c ƒë·ªãnh $U[0.01, 0.1]$.
4. **Misalignment**: M√¥ ph·ªèng **sai l·ªách camera extrinsic**:
    - Perturbation trong g√≥c xoay [‚àí0.5¬∞, 0.5¬∞] ƒë·∫øn [‚àí2¬∞, 2¬∞].
    - Perturbation trong d·ªãch chuy·ªÉn [‚àí0.005, 0.005] ƒë·∫øn [‚àí0.02, 0.02].
5. **Missing points**: M√¥ ph·ªèng m·∫•t ƒëi·ªÉm b·∫±ng c√°ch gi·ªõi h·∫°n **viewing positions** trong c√°c d·∫£i g√≥c nh·ªè `polar angle`:
    - D·∫£i g√≥c gi·∫£m `scanned surface areas` t·ª´ **99% (3 trajectories)** xu·ªëng **86% (1 trajectory)** t√πy m·ª©c ƒë·ªô thi·∫øu ƒëi·ªÉm.

## **The Synthetic Data of Scene Surfaces**

![Screenshot 2024-11-23 at 18.37.49.png](Surface%20Reconstruction%20From%20Point%20Clouds%20A%20Survey%20%201442a3f8f2a180aca990fd4b2793fb3b/Screenshot_2024-11-23_at_18.37.49.png)

Ph·∫ßn n√†y m·ªü r·ªông quy tr√¨nh t·∫°o d·ªØ li·ªáu t·ªïng h·ª£p t·ª´ c·∫•p ƒë·ªô **object surfaces** (m√¥ h√¨nh ƒë·ªëi t∆∞·ª£ng) sang **scene surfaces** (m√¥ h√¨nh c·∫£nh), v·ªõi m·ª•c ti√™u m√¥ ph·ªèng vi·ªác qu√©t b·ªÅ m·∫∑t trong c√°c m√¥i tr∆∞·ªùng th·ª±c t·∫ø quy m√¥ l·ªõn h∆°n. T√°c gi·∫£ x√¢y d·ª±ng d·ªØ li·ªáu c·∫•p ƒë·ªô c·∫£nh v·ªõi ƒë·∫ßy ƒë·ªß c√°c d·∫°ng l·ªói ph·ªï bi·∫øn trong qu√° tr√¨nh qu√©t th·ª±c t·∫ø, bao g·ªìm **point-wise noise**, **point outliers**, **non-uniform distribution of points**, **misalignment**, v√† **missing points**. Ph·∫ßn n√†y ƒë∆∞·ª£c m√¥ t·∫£ chi ti·∫øt qua c√°c b∆∞·ªõc t·ª´ thu th·∫≠p d·ªØ li·ªáu ƒë·∫øn qu√©t t·ªïng h·ª£p, ƒë∆∞·ª£c ph√¢n t√≠ch b√™n d∆∞·ªõi.

### **1. Thu th·∫≠p d·ªØ li·ªáu CAD cho Scene Surfaces**

**Ngu·ªìn d·ªØ li·ªáu:** T√°c gi·∫£ thu th·∫≠p **CAD surface models** t·ª´ ba b·ªô d·ªØ li·ªáu ph·ªï bi·∫øn, ƒë·∫£m b·∫£o t√≠nh ƒëa d·∫°ng v·ªÅ lo·∫°i ph√≤ng, k√≠ch th∆∞·ªõc, n·ªôi th·∫•t, v√† v·∫≠t d·ª•ng:

- **SceneNet [24]**: Ch·ªçn ng·∫´u nhi√™n **28 c·∫£nh**.
- **3D-FRONT [25]**: Ch·ªçn **14 c·∫£nh**.
- **Replica [29]**: Ch·ªçn **8 c·∫£nh**.

**ƒê·∫∑c ƒëi·ªÉm d·ªØ li·ªáu (T∆∞∆°ng t·ª± nh∆∞ object)**

- C√°c **meshes** ƒë∆∞·ª£c th·ªÉ hi·ªán d∆∞·ªõi d·∫°ng **triangular meshes** ƒë·ªÉ ƒë·∫£m b·∫£o t√≠nh nh·∫•t qu√°n v·ªõi d·ªØ li·ªáu c·∫•p ƒë·ªô ƒë·ªëi t∆∞·ª£ng.
- **Chu·∫©n h√≥a**:
    - **CƒÉn gi·ªØa t·∫°i g·ªëc t·ªça ƒë·ªô (origin)**: ƒê·∫£m b·∫£o m·ªói c·∫£nh ƒë∆∞·ª£c ƒë·ªãnh v·ªã ·ªü trung t√¢m kh√¥ng gian.
    - **Gi·ªØ nguy√™n k√≠ch th∆∞·ªõc g·ªëc**: Kh√¥ng co gi√£n k√≠ch th∆∞·ªõc nh∆∞ c·∫•p ƒë·ªô object.

**√ù nghƒ©a:** Vi·ªác thu th·∫≠p t·ª´ c√°c b·ªô d·ªØ li·ªáu tr√™n gi√∫p t·∫°o ra c√°c c·∫£nh th·ª±c t·∫ø ƒëa d·∫°ng, ph·∫£n √°nh nhi·ªÅu lo·∫°i m√¥i tr∆∞·ªùng trong nh√†.

### **2. Quy tr√¨nh qu√©t t·ªïng h·ª£p cho Scene Surfaces**

**S·ª≠ d·ª•ng c√¥ng c·ª• qu√©t**

- C√¥ng c·ª• qu√©t t·ªïng h·ª£p: **Blender Sensor Simulation Toolbox (BlenSor)** [137].
- C·∫£m bi·∫øn m√¥ ph·ªèng: **Kinect V2** [140] v·ªõi kho·∫£ng c√°ch l√†m vi·ªác t·ª´ **0.75m ƒë·∫øn 2.1m**, ph√π h·ª£p v·ªõi c√°c m√¥i tr∆∞·ªùng trong nh√†.

**C√†i ƒë·∫∑t qu√©t**

1. **CƒÉn ch·ªânh v√† ƒë·ªãnh v·ªã scene**: ƒê·∫∑t mesh c·ªßa **scene** v√†o **kh√¥ng gian 3D ƒë∆∞·ª£c gi·ªõi h·∫°n**:
    - K√≠ch th∆∞·ªõc kh√¥ng gian: Bao tr·ªçn to√†n b·ªô b·ªÅ m·∫∑t c·ªßa c·∫£nh.
    - T√¢m c·ªßa c·∫£nh ƒë∆∞·ª£c ƒë·∫∑t t·∫°i g·ªëc t·ªça ƒë·ªô.
2. **Ph√¢n chia kh√¥ng gian**:
    - Kh√¥ng gian 3D ƒë∆∞·ª£c chia th√†nh c√°c kh·ªëi l·∫≠p ph∆∞∆°ng **k√≠ch th∆∞·ªõc 1m¬≥**, ch·ªìng l·∫•n nhau **0.5m¬≥**.
    - M·ªôt s·ªë kh·ªëi c√≥ th·ªÉ r·ªóng (kh√¥ng ch·ª©a b·ªÅ m·∫∑t), trong khi nh·ªØng kh·ªëi kh√°c ch·ª©a c√°c m·∫£nh b·ªÅ m·∫∑t c·ªßa c·∫£nh.
3. **ƒê·∫∑t camera t·∫°i c√°c v·ªã tr√≠ kh·ªëi r·ªóng**:
    - Ch·ªçn **t√¢m c·ªßa c√°c kh·ªëi r·ªóng** l√†m v·ªã tr√≠ ƒë·∫∑t camera, ƒë·∫£m b·∫£o camera n·∫±m trong kho·∫£ng c√°ch l√†m vi·ªác c·ªßa Kinect V2.
    - Camera c√≥ th·ªÉ qu√©t c√°c ph·∫ßn b·ªÅ m·∫∑t t·ª´ **nhi·ªÅu h∆∞·ªõng kh√°c nhau** tr√™n m·ªôt h√¨nh c·∫ßu quan s√°t (viewing sphere) xu·∫•t ph√°t t·ª´ t√¢m c·ªßa kh·ªëi r·ªóng.
4. **L·∫•y m·∫´u ng·∫´u nhi√™n c√°c h∆∞·ªõng qu√©t**:
    - T·∫°i m·ªói v·ªã tr√≠, ch·ªçn ng·∫´u nhi√™n **100 h∆∞·ªõng qu√©t** ƒë·ªÉ thi·∫øt l·∫≠p c√°c th√¥ng s·ªë camera **extrinsics** :
        
        $$
        K_{ij} = [R_j | t_i]
        $$
        
        - $R_j$: Ma tr·∫≠n xoay (rotation matrix).
        - $t_i$: V·ªã tr√≠ camera.
5. **T√≠ch h·ª£p c√°c point clouds**: T·∫°o ra **c√°c point clouds c·ª•c b·ªô** t·ª´ m·ªói h∆∞·ªõng qu√©t $K_{ij} \circ P_{K_{ij}}$, sau ƒë√≥ registeraion v√† h·ª£p nh·∫•t ch√∫ng ƒë·ªÉ t·∫°o th√†nh point cloud $P$ cu·ªëi c√πng .

<aside>
üí°

**Kh√¥ng √°p d·ª•ng Farthest Point Sampling (FPS)**: Kh√°c v·ªõi level of object, ·ªü c·∫•p ƒë·ªô scences kh√¥ng √°p d·ª•ng FPS, d·∫´n ƒë·∫øn hi·ªán t∆∞·ª£ng **non-uniform distribution** (ph√¢n b·ªë kh√¥ng ƒë·ªìng ƒë·ªÅu) x·∫£y ra t·ª± nhi√™n.

</aside>

**T√≠nh to√°n surface normals**: 

- C√°c **surface normals** ƒë∆∞·ª£c t√≠nh theo c√°ch t∆∞∆°ng t·ª± nh∆∞ trong ph·∫ßn **object scanning.**
- D·ª±a tr√™n **PCA** t·ª´ 40 ƒëi·ªÉm l√¢n c·∫≠n g·∫ßn nh·∫•t c·ªßa m·ªói ƒëi·ªÉm.

### **3. M√¥ ph·ªèng c√°c th√°ch th·ª©c trong qu√©t th·ª±c t·∫ø**

C≈©ng nh∆∞ complex of objects, d·ªØ li·ªáu t·ªïng h·ª£p complex of **scene** m√¥ ph·ªèng **5 main challenges** th∆∞·ªùng g·∫∑p trong th·ª±c t·∫ø:

**1) Non-uniform distribution of points**: **T·ª± nhi√™n xu·∫•t hi·ªán** do kh√¥ng √°p d·ª•ng FPS, d·∫´n ƒë·∫øn m·∫≠t ƒë·ªô ƒëi·ªÉm kh√¥ng ƒë·ªìng ƒë·ªÅu gi·ªØa c√°c v√πng b·ªÅ m·∫∑t.

**2) Missing points**: Xu·∫•t hi·ªán t·ª± nhi√™n do **self-occlusion** (che khu·∫•t b·∫£n th√¢n) v√† g√≥c quan s√°t h·∫°n ch·∫ø c·ªßa camera.

**3) Point-wise noise**: M√¥ ph·ªèng nhi·ªÖu ƒëi·ªÉm ƒë·ªôc l·∫≠p: Nhi·ªÖu Gaussian v·ªõi ƒë·ªô l·ªách chu·∫©n $\sigma_{\text{noise}} = 0.005m$

**4) Point outliers**: Th√™m c√°c ƒëi·ªÉm outliers b·∫±ng c√°ch d·ªãch chuy·ªÉn m·ªôt t·ª∑ l·ªá $_{\text{outlier}} = 0.4\%$ c·ªßa c√°c ƒëi·ªÉm. D·ªãch chuy·ªÉn ng·∫´u nhi√™n trong kho·∫£ng $[a_{\text{outlier}}, b_{\text{outlier}}] = [0.01m, 0.1m]$.

**5) Misalignment**: M√¥ ph·ªèng sai l·ªách c·ªßa **camera extrinsic**:

- Perturbation trong g√≥c xoay: $[a_{\text{rotation}}, b_{\text{rotation}}] = [-1.5^\circ, 1.5^\circ]$
- Perturbation trong d·ªãch chuy·ªÉn: $[a_{\text{translation}}, b_{\text{translation}}] = [-0.015m, 0.015m]$

### **4. K·∫øt qu·∫£ c·ªßa d·ªØ li·ªáu qu√©t t·ªïng h·ª£p**

**Quy m√¥ c·ªßa point cloud cu·ªëi c√πng:** Point cloud c·ªßa m·ªói c·∫£nh ch·ª©a kho·∫£ng **1 tri·ªáu ƒëi·ªÉm**, bao g·ªìm ƒë·∫ßy ƒë·ªß c·∫£ **5 challenges**.

**√ù nghƒ©a c·ªßa d·ªØ li·ªáu c·∫•p ƒë·ªô c·∫£nh**

- Ph·∫£n √°nh c√°c ƒëi·ªÅu ki·ªán th·ª±c t·∫ø c·ªßa vi·ªác qu√©t m√¥i tr∆∞·ªùng trong nh√† v·ªõi quy m√¥ l·ªõn.
- D·ªØ li·ªáu n√†y h·ªó tr·ª£ ƒë√°nh gi√° hi·ªáu qu·∫£ c√°c ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p t√°i t·∫°o b·ªÅ m·∫∑t trong c√°c ƒëi·ªÅu ki·ªán th·ª±c t·∫ø ph·ª©c t·∫°p h∆°n so v·ªõi c·∫•p ƒë·ªô ƒë·ªëi t∆∞·ª£ng.

## **Section C: The Real-Scanned Data**

![Screenshot 2024-11-23 at 18.38.02.png](Surface%20Reconstruction%20From%20Point%20Clouds%20A%20Survey%20%201442a3f8f2a180aca990fd4b2793fb3b/Screenshot_2024-11-23_at_18.38.02.png)

Ph·∫ßn n√†y t·∫≠p trung v√†o d·ªØ li·ªáu qu√©t th·ª±c t·∫ø (**real-scanned data**) ƒë∆∞·ª£c x√¢y d·ª±ng ƒë·ªÉ h·ªó tr·ª£ ƒë√°nh gi√° c√°c ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p t√°i t·∫°o b·ªÅ m·∫∑t trong **benchmark**. T√°c gi·∫£ m√¥ t·∫£ quy tr√¨nh qu√©t c√°c ƒë·ªëi t∆∞·ª£ng th·ª±c b·∫±ng hai lo·∫°i camera qu√©t 3D c√≥ ƒë·ªô ch√≠nh x√°c kh√°c nhau, nh·∫±m t·∫°o ra d·ªØ li·ªáu ƒë·∫ßu v√†o v√† d·ªØ li·ªáu g·∫ßn ƒë√∫ng v·ªõi ground-truth. D∆∞·ªõi ƒë√¢y l√† ph√¢n t√≠ch chi ti·∫øt t·ª´ng n·ªôi dung ch√≠nh c·ªßa ph·∫ßn n√†y.

### **1. T·ªïng quan v·ªÅ d·ªØ li·ªáu qu√©t th·ª±c t·∫ø**

**M·ª•c ti√™u**

- **T·∫°o d·ªØ li·ªáu qu√©t th·ª±c t·∫ø** t·ª´ c√°c ƒë·ªëi t∆∞·ª£ng th·∫≠t ƒë·ªÉ b·ªï sung cho d·ªØ li·ªáu t·ªïng h·ª£p ƒë√£ ƒë∆∞·ª£c m√¥ t·∫£ tr∆∞·ªõc ƒë√≥.
- Bao g·ªìm hai lo·∫°i point clouds:
    - **Input point cloud**: ƒê∆∞·ª£c qu√©t b·ªüi camera c√≥ ƒë·ªô ch√≠nh x√°c th·∫•p h∆°n, m√¥ ph·ªèng d·ªØ li·ªáu qu√©t ƒë·∫ßu v√†o th·ª±c t·∫ø.
    - **Ground-truth point cloud**: ƒê∆∞·ª£c qu√©t b·ªüi camera c√≥ ƒë·ªô ch√≠nh x√°c cao, s·ª≠ d·ª•ng l√†m ƒëi·ªÉm tham chi·∫øu (ground-truth) ƒë·ªÉ ƒë√°nh gi√°.

### **2. Thi·∫øt b·ªã v√† th√¥ng s·ªë k·ªπ thu·∫≠t**

**Thi·∫øt b·ªã qu√©t**

1. **SHINING 3D Einscan SE3**:
    - ƒê·ªô ch√≠nh x√°c: **100 micromet**.
    - D√πng ƒë·ªÉ t·∫°o **input point cloud**.
2. **SHINING 3D OKIO 5 M4**:
    - ƒê·ªô ch√≠nh x√°c: **5 micromet**.
    - D√πng ƒë·ªÉ t·∫°o **ground-truth point cloud**.

**Quy tr√¨nh x·ª≠ l√Ω ground-truth**

- Ground-truth ƒë∆∞·ª£c x√¢y d·ª±ng t·ª´ c√°c point clouds qu√©t b·ªüi OKIO 5 M4, thay v√¨ chuy·ªÉn ƒë·ªïi ch√∫ng th√†nh surface meshes b·∫±ng ph·∫ßn m·ªÅm t√≠ch h·ª£p s·∫µn.
- **L√Ω do**: ƒê√°nh gi√° t√°i t·∫°o b·ªÅ m·∫∑t s·ª≠ d·ª•ng c√°c **metrics v·ªÅ kho·∫£ng c√°ch gi·ªØa c√°c t·∫≠p ƒëi·ªÉm (point set distances)**, v√¨ v·∫≠y s·ª≠ d·ª•ng raw point clouds l√† h·ª£p l√Ω v√† tr·ª±c ti·∫øp h∆°n.

### **3. Thu th·∫≠p d·ªØ li·ªáu**

**ƒê·ªëi t∆∞·ª£ng ƒë∆∞·ª£c qu√©t**

T√°c gi·∫£ qu√©t **20 ƒë·ªëi t∆∞·ª£ng th·ª±c** v·ªõi c√°c ƒë·∫∑c ƒëi·ªÉm ƒëa d·∫°ng:

- **ƒê·ªô ph·ª©c t·∫°p b·ªÅ m·∫∑t**: G·ªìm c√°c nh√≥m nh∆∞ h√†ng h√≥a (**commodities**), c√¥ng c·ª• (**instruments**), v√† t√°c ph·∫©m ngh·ªá thu·∫≠t (**artwares**).
- **V·∫≠t li·ªáu b·ªÅ m·∫∑t**: Kim lo·∫°i (**metal**), nh·ª±a (**plastic**), g·ªëm (**ceramic**), v√† v·∫£i (**cloth**).

**L√Ω do l·ª±a ch·ªçn ƒëa d·∫°ng ƒë·ªëi t∆∞·ª£ng v√† v·∫≠t li·ªáu v√¨ T√≠nh ƒë·∫°i di·ªán cao**: ƒê·∫£m b·∫£o r·∫±ng c√°c ƒëi·ªÅu ki·ªán kh√¥ng ho√†n h·∫£o trong qu√©t th·ª±c t·∫ø (imperfections) nh∆∞ ph·∫£n x·∫° √°nh s√°ng, che khu·∫•t, v√† ph√¢n b·ªë kh√¥ng ƒë·ªìng ƒë·ªÅu ƒë∆∞·ª£c m√¥ ph·ªèng ƒë·∫ßy ƒë·ªß.

**V√≠ d·ª• minh h·ªça**

- C√°c ƒë·ªëi t∆∞·ª£ng th·ª±c t·∫ø ƒë∆∞·ª£c hi·ªÉn th·ªã trong **H√¨nh 5** c·ªßa b√†i vi·∫øt.
- **H√¨nh 6** minh h·ªça c√°c c·∫∑p d·ªØ li·ªáu qu√©t (input vs. ground-truth) t·ª´ hai lo·∫°i camera.

### **4. Quy tr√¨nh qu√©t th·ª±c t·∫ø**

**Qu√©t t·ª´ nhi·ªÅu g√≥c nh√¨n**

- Ch·∫•t l∆∞·ª£ng point clouds ƒë∆∞·ª£c c·∫£i thi·ªán khi tƒÉng s·ªë l·∫ßn qu√©t t·ª´ c√°c g√≥c nh√¨n kh√°c nhau (**multi-view scanning**).
- **H√¨nh 4** cho th·∫•y m·ªëi quan h·ªá gi·ªØa s·ªë l∆∞·ª£ng g√≥c qu√©t v√† ch·ªâ s·ªë **Chamfer Distances (CD)**: CD gi·∫£m khi s·ªë l∆∞·ª£ng g√≥c qu√©t tƒÉng, nh∆∞ng ƒë·∫°t ƒë·∫øn ng∆∞·ª°ng b√£o h√≤a sau m·ªôt s·ªë l∆∞·ª£ng nh·∫•t ƒë·ªãnh.

**S·ªë l∆∞·ª£ng g√≥c qu√©t t·ªëi ∆∞u**

- **Einscan SE**: S·ª≠ d·ª•ng kho·∫£ng **40 g√≥c qu√©t** ƒë·ªÉ ƒë·∫°t ch·∫•t l∆∞·ª£ng t·ªëi ∆∞u.
- **OKIO 5 M**: S·ª≠ d·ª•ng kho·∫£ng **20 g√≥c qu√©t** ƒë·ªÉ ƒë·∫°t ch·∫•t l∆∞·ª£ng t·ªëi ∆∞u.

**C√¥ng c·ª• x·ª≠ l√Ω:** Sau khi qu√©t, c√°c point clouds t·ª´ c√°c g√≥c qu√©t kh√°c nhau ƒë∆∞·ª£c cƒÉn ch·ªânh (**registration**) v√† h·ª£p nh·∫•t b·∫±ng ph·∫ßn m·ªÅm **CloudCompare [141]**.

### **5. ƒê·∫∑c ƒëi·ªÉm d·ªØ li·ªáu qu√©t th·ª±c t·∫ø**

**ƒê·∫∑c ƒëi·ªÉm n·ªïi b·∫≠t:** C√°c point clouds ƒë·∫ßu v√†o c√≥ th·ªÉ ch·ª©a c√°c l·ªói qu√©t th·ª±c t·∫ø, nh∆∞:

- Nhi·ªÖu (**noise**).
- ƒêi·ªÉm ngo·∫°i lai (**outliers**).
- Sai l·ªách do cƒÉn ch·ªânh (**misalignment**).

**Th√¥ng s·ªë chi ti·∫øt**

- **S·ªë l∆∞·ª£ng ƒë·ªëi t∆∞·ª£ng**: 20.
- **Camera Einscan SE**:
    - Input point clouds.
    - ƒê·ªô ch√≠nh x√°c: 100 micromet.
    - 40 g√≥c qu√©t.
- **Camera OKIO 5 M**:
    - Ground-truth point clouds.
    - ƒê·ªô ch√≠nh x√°c: 5 micromet.
    - 20 g√≥c qu√©t.

**‚Üí Th·ªëng k√™ d·ªØ li·ªáu:** C√°c th√¥ng s·ªë chi ti·∫øt c·ªßa b·ªô d·ªØ li·ªáu qu√©t th·ª±c t·∫ø ƒë∆∞·ª£c tr√¨nh b√†y trong **B·∫£ng IV**.

### **6. M·ª•c ti√™u c·ªßa b·ªô d·ªØ li·ªáu qu√©t th·ª±c t·∫ø**

**ƒê√°nh gi√° ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p t√°i t·∫°o b·ªÅ m·∫∑t**

- Cung c·∫•p d·ªØ li·ªáu th·ª±c t·∫ø ƒë·ªÉ ki·ªÉm tra hi·ªáu nƒÉng c·ªßa c√°c ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p trong ƒëi·ªÅu ki·ªán th·ª±c t·∫ø.
- ƒê·∫£m b·∫£o r·∫±ng d·ªØ li·ªáu ƒë·∫°i di·ªán cho c√°c l·ªói qu√©t ph·ªï bi·∫øn trong th·ª±c t·∫ø.

**So s√°nh v·ªõi d·ªØ li·ªáu t·ªïng h·ª£p**

- D·ªØ li·ªáu t·ªïng h·ª£p m√¥ ph·ªèng c√°c l·ªói qu√©t trong m√¥i tr∆∞·ªùng gi·∫£ l·∫≠p.
- D·ªØ li·ªáu th·ª±c t·∫ø ki·ªÉm tra kh·∫£ nƒÉng √°p d·ª•ng ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p trong ƒëi·ªÅu ki·ªán th·ª±c t·∫ø v·ªõi c√°c v·∫≠t li·ªáu v√† ƒë·ªëi t∆∞·ª£ng ph·ª©c t·∫°p.

---

## **EXPERIMENTAL SET-UP FOR BENCHMARKING EXISTING SURFACE RECONSTRUCTION METHODS**

Section n√†y tr√¨nh b√†y c√°ch thi·∫øt l·∫≠p th·ª±c nghi·ªám nh·∫±m **ƒë√°nh gi√° c√°c surface reconstruction hi·ªán c√≥** th√¥ng qua m·ªôt b·ªô d·ªØ li·ªáu chu·∫©n (benchmark). T√°c gi·∫£ m√¥ t·∫£ c√°ch t·ªï ch·ª©c d·ªØ li·ªáu, quy tr√¨nh ti·ªÅn x·ª≠ l√Ω, c√°c ti√™u ch√≠ ƒë√°nh gi√° v√† c√°c ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p ƒë∆∞·ª£c ch·ªçn ƒë·ªÉ th·ª≠ nghi·ªám. M·ª•c ti√™u l√† x√°c ƒë·ªãnh ∆∞u, nh∆∞·ª£c ƒëi·ªÉm c·ªßa c√°c ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p trong c√°c ƒëi·ªÅu ki·ªán kh√°c nhau.

### **A. D·ªØ li·ªáu s·ª≠ d·ª•ng trong th·ª≠ nghi·ªám**

**1. D·ªØ li·ªáu t·ª´ benchmark**

T·ª´ b·ªô d·ªØ li·ªáu ƒë∆∞·ª£c x√¢y d·ª±ng ·ªü Section IV, t√°c gi·∫£ ch·ªçn m·ªôt t·∫≠p con `subset` ƒë·ªÉ th·ª±c hi·ªán th·ª≠ nghi·ªám:

- **22 surfaces t·ªïng h·ª£p c·ªßa c√°c object instances**:
    - Ph√¢n b·ªë: **12 b·ªÅ m·∫∑t c√≥ ƒë·ªô ph·ª©c t·∫°p th·∫•p**, **6 trung b√¨nh**, **4 cao**.
    - M·ªói b·ªÅ m·∫∑t ƒë∆∞·ª£c qu√©t theo **6 c√°ch** (bao g·ªìm qu√©t ho√†n h·∫£o `perfect scaning` v√† c√°c l·ªói qu√©t kh√°c nhau), t·∫°o th√†nh **308 c·∫∑p input-output** cho benchmarking.
- **50 b·ªÅ m·∫∑t c·∫£nh t·ªïng h·ª£p (synthetic scene surfaces)**.
- **20 b·ªÅ m·∫∑t qu√©t th·ª±c t·∫ø (real-scanned surfaces)**.

**2. D·ªØ li·ªáu b·ªï tr·ª£ cho ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p h·ªçc s√¢u**

V·ªõi c√°c ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p d·ª±a tr√™n **learning-based priors**, t√°c gi·∫£ c·∫ßn m·ªôt t·∫≠p d·ªØ li·ªáu b·ªï tr·ª£ `aulixiary dataset` ƒë·ªÉ hu·∫•n luy·ªán c√°c m√¥ h√¨nh:

- **ShapeNet [18] v√† ABC [21]**: C√°c surfaces t·ª´ c√°c ngu·ªìn n√†y ƒë∆∞·ª£c d√πng ƒë·ªÉ hu·∫•n luy·ªán.
- **D·ªØ li·ªáu c√≤n l·∫°i trong benchmark**: S·ª≠ d·ª•ng c√°c d·ªØ li·ªáu kh√¥ng ƒë∆∞·ª£c ch·ªçn v√†o t·∫≠p th·ª≠ nghi·ªám.

‚Üí T√°c gi·∫£ ti·∫øn h√†nh hu·∫•n luy·ªán l·∫°i (retrain) **OccNet [9]** v√† **DeepSDF [8]** tr√™n t·∫≠p d·ªØ li·ªáu b·ªï tr·ª£ n√†y (chi ti·∫øt trong Appendix C).

### **B. Ti·ªÅn x·ª≠ l√Ω d·ªØ li·ªáu**

Quy tr√¨nh ti·ªÅn x·ª≠ l√Ω ƒë∆∞·ª£c th·ª±c hi·ªán tr∆∞·ªõc khi √°p d·ª•ng c√°c ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p t√°i t·∫°o b·ªÅ m·∫∑t, nh·∫±m c·∫£i thi·ªán hi·ªáu nƒÉng. T√°c gi·∫£ so s√°nh hi·ªáu nƒÉng c·ªßa c√°c ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p **c√≥** v√† **kh√¥ng c√≥ ti·ªÅn x·ª≠ l√Ω**.

**1. Quy tr√¨nh ti·ªÅn x·ª≠ l√Ω d·ªØ li·ªáu t·ªïng h·ª£p**

- **Outlier removal (lo·∫°i b·ªè outliers)**:
    - S·ª≠ d·ª•ng ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p th·ªëng k√™ [142].
    - Quy t·∫Øc: M·ªôt ƒëi·ªÉm $p \in P$ ƒë∆∞·ª£c coi l√† outlier n·∫øu **kho·∫£ng c√°ch trung b√¨nh $\bar{d}_p$** c·ªßa n√≥ ƒë·∫øn $k = 35$ ƒëi·ªÉm l√¢n c·∫≠n l·ªõn h∆°n $5 \cdot \sigma_{\bar{d}}$ (ƒë·ªô l·ªách chu·∫©n c·ªßa kho·∫£ng c√°ch trung b√¨nh tr√™n to√†n b·ªô point cloud $P$).
- **De-noising (kh·ª≠ nhi·ªÖu)**:
    - S·ª≠ d·ª•ng **Jets smoothing [143]**:
        - Fit m·ªôt b·ªÅ m·∫∑t tham s·ªë c·ª•c b·ªô v√†o l√¢n c·∫≠n c·ªßa ƒëi·ªÉm.
        - D·ª±ng l·∫°i c√°c ƒëi·ªÉm $\{p \in N\}$ b·∫±ng c√°ch chi·∫øu ch√∫ng l√™n b·ªÅ m·∫∑t ƒë∆∞·ª£c fit.
        - S·ªë l∆∞·ª£ng l√¢n c·∫≠n: $k = 18$.
- **Point re-sampling (l·∫•y m·∫´u l·∫°i ƒëi·ªÉm)**:
    - S·ª≠ d·ª•ng **Farthest Point Sampling (FPS) [106]** ƒë·ªÉ t·∫°o ph√¢n b·ªë ƒëi·ªÉm ƒë·ªìng ƒë·ªÅu h∆°n.
    - Gi·∫£m s·ªë l∆∞·ª£ng ƒëi·ªÉm c√≤n **40%** c·ªßa t·∫≠p ban ƒë·∫ßu.

**2. Ti·ªÅn x·ª≠ l√Ω d·ªØ li·ªáu qu√©t th·ª±c t·∫ø**

- S·ª≠ d·ª•ng c√¥ng c·ª• ti·ªÅn x·ª≠ l√Ω t√≠ch h·ª£p c·ªßa c√°c m√°y qu√©t.
- Sau ƒë√≥ th·ª±c hi·ªán b∆∞·ªõc cu·ªëi: **FPS ƒë·ªÉ l·∫•y m·∫´u l·∫°i 200,000 ƒëi·ªÉm cho m·ªói point cloud**.

### **C. C√°c ti√™u ch√≠ ƒë√°nh gi√° (Evaluation Metrics)**

T√°c gi·∫£ s·ª≠ d·ª•ng 4 ti√™u ch√≠ ch√≠nh ƒë·ªÉ ƒë·ªãnh l∆∞·ª£ng v√† so s√°nh k·∫øt qu·∫£ t√°i t·∫°o:

**1. Chamfer Distance (CD) [145]**

- ƒêo **kho·∫£ng c√°ch trung b√¨nh** t·ª´ c√°c ƒëi·ªÉm tr√™n b·ªÅ m·∫∑t t√°i t·∫°o ƒë·∫øn b·ªÅ m·∫∑t g·ªëc v√† ng∆∞·ª£c l·∫°i.
- **√ù nghƒ©a**: ƒêo ƒë·ªô t∆∞∆°ng ƒë·ªìng h√¨nh d·∫°ng t·ªïng th·ªÉ gi·ªØa b·ªÅ m·∫∑t t√°i t·∫°o v√† b·ªÅ m·∫∑t g·ªëc.

**2. F-Score [146]**

- ƒê√°nh gi√° ƒë·ªô ch√≠nh x√°c v√† ƒë·ªô bao ph·ªß:
    - Precision: T·ª∑ l·ªá c√°c ƒëi·ªÉm t√°i t·∫°o n·∫±m g·∫ßn b·ªÅ m·∫∑t g·ªëc.
    - Recall: T·ª∑ l·ªá c√°c ƒëi·ªÉm b·ªÅ m·∫∑t g·ªëc n·∫±m g·∫ßn b·ªÅ m·∫∑t t√°i t·∫°o.
- **√ù nghƒ©a**: ƒêo l∆∞·ªùng kh·∫£ nƒÉng t√°i t·∫°o b·ªÅ m·∫∑t ƒë√∫ng v√† ƒë·∫ßy ƒë·ªß.

**3. Normal Consistency Score (NCS) [9]**

- ƒêo ƒë·ªô nh·∫•t qu√°n gi·ªØa c√°c ph√°p tuy·∫øn tr√™n b·ªÅ m·∫∑t t√°i t·∫°o v√† b·ªÅ m·∫∑t g·ªëc.
- **√ù nghƒ©a**: ƒê√°nh gi√° chi ti·∫øt c·ª•c b·ªô, ƒë·∫∑c bi·ªát quan tr·ªçng v·ªõi c√°c ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p c·∫ßn gi·ªØ ƒë∆∞·ª£c ƒë·ªô tr∆°n c·ªßa b·ªÅ m·∫∑t.

**4. Neural Feature Similarity (NFS)**

- **ƒê·ªÅ xu·∫•t m·ªõi**: D·ª±a tr√™n s·ª± t∆∞∆°ng ƒë·ªìng c·ªßa hai b·ªÅ m·∫∑t trong kh√¥ng gian ƒë·∫∑c tr∆∞ng s√¢u (**deep feature space**).
- **√ù nghƒ©a**: ƒê√°nh gi√° s·ª± kh√°c bi·ªát ·ªü m·ª©c ƒë·ªô ng·ªØ nghƒ©a (semantic) g·∫ßn g≈©i v·ªõi nh·∫≠n th·ª©c c·ªßa con ng∆∞·ªùi.

**So s√°nh NFS v·ªõi Light Field Distance (LFD) [148]**:

- Gi·ªëng nhau: C·∫£ hai ƒë·ªÅu c√≥ kh·∫£ nƒÉng n·∫Øm b·∫Øt c√°c chi ti·∫øt t·ª´ th√¥ ƒë·∫øn m·ªãn c·ªßa h√¨nh d·∫°ng.
- Kh√°c nhau:
    - **NFS**: √Åp d·ª•ng ƒë∆∞·ª£c cho t·∫•t c·∫£ c√°c lo·∫°i d·ªØ li·ªáu (synthetic v√† real-scanned).
    - **LFD**: Ch·ªâ √°p d·ª•ng ƒë∆∞·ª£c cho c√°c b·ªÅ m·∫∑t t·ªïng h·ª£p ·ªü c·∫•p ƒë·ªô ƒë·ªëi t∆∞·ª£ng (synthetic object-level surfaces).

### **D. C√°c ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p ƒë∆∞·ª£c ch·ªçn v√† c√°ch tri·ªÉn khai**

**1. Ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p ƒë∆∞·ª£c ch·ªçn**

D·ª±a tr√™n c√°c **geometric priors** ƒë√£ ph√¢n lo·∫°i trong Section III-E, t√°c gi·∫£ ch·ªçn c√°c ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p ƒë·∫°i di·ªán t·ª´ m·ªói nh√≥m:

- **Triangulation-based prior**:
    - **GD [41]**.
    - **BPA [42]**.
- **Surface smoothness prior**:
    - **SPSR [39]**: D·ª±a tr√™n chi·∫øn l∆∞·ª£c ƒëi·ªÅu chu·∫©n b·∫≠c hai (cf. Eq. (10)).
    - **RIMLS [63]**: K·∫øt h·ª£p c·∫£ hai chi·∫øn l∆∞·ª£c ƒëi·ªÅu chu·∫©n (cf. Eq. (9)).
- **Modeling prior**:
    - **SALD [83]**: D√†nh cho point clouds kh√¥ng ƒë·ªãnh h∆∞·ªõng (un-oriented).
    - **IGR [37]**: D√†nh cho point clouds c√≥ ƒë·ªãnh h∆∞·ªõng (oriented).
- **Learning-based prior**:
    - **OccNet [9]**, **DeepSDF [8]**: H·ªçc ƒë·∫∑c tr∆∞ng h√¨nh d·∫°ng to√†n c·ª•c (global learning).
    - **LIG [10]**, **Points2Surf [89]**: H·ªçc ƒë·∫∑c tr∆∞ng c·ª•c b·ªô (local learning).
- **Hybrid priors**:
    - **DSE [123]**: K·∫øt h·ª£p triangulation-based v√† learning-based priors.
    - **IMLSNet [124]**: K·∫øt h·ª£p surface smoothness v√† learning-based priors.
    - **ParseNet [47]**: K·∫øt h·ª£p template-based v√† learning-based priors.

<aside>
üí°

T√°c gi·∫£ kh√¥ng s·ª≠ d·ª•ng ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p template-based prior b·ªüi v√¨ performance ph·∫ßn l·ªõn ph·ª• thu·ªôc v√†o assumed templates v√† kh√≥ ƒë·ªÉ reconstruct b·ªÅ m·∫∑t ph·ª©c t·∫°p.

</aside>

**2. C√°ch tri·ªÉn khai**

- **C√°c ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p kh√¥ng d·ª±a tr√™n h·ªçc s√¢u (classical methods)**:
    - **GD**: D√πng th∆∞ vi·ªán **CGAL [149]**.
    - **BPA, SPSR, RIMLS**: S·ª≠ d·ª•ng **MeshLab [150]** v·ªõi ƒëi·ªÅu ch·ªânh tham s·ªë ph√π h·ª£p.
- **C√°c ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p h·ªçc s√¢u (learning-based methods)**:
    - S·ª≠ d·ª•ng code ƒë∆∞·ª£c c√¥ng b·ªë ch√≠nh th·ª©c c·ªßa t√°c gi·∫£ (n·∫øu c√≥).
    - V·ªõi c√°c ph∆∞∆°ng ph√°p kh√¥ng c√≥ m√£ ngu·ªìn, t√°c gi·∫£ tri·ªÉn khai l·∫°i (re-implement) v√† tinh ch·ªânh hyper-parameters.
